vyāsakṛtam
yasyā''jñayā jagatsraṣṭā virañciḥ pālako hāraḥ
tīrthānāmuttamaṃ tīrtha kṣetrāṇāṃ kṣetramuttamam
munīnāmāśrayo nityaṃ naimiṣāraṇyamuttamam
śaunakādyā mahātmānaḥ śivabhaktā mahaujasaḥ
tasminsatre mahābhāgo munīnāṃ bhāgyagauravāt
ājagāma munīndraṣṭuṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā te mahātmāno naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ
prahṛṣṭāḥ praśumudyuktāḥ papracchū romaharṣaṇam
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ bhagavatā pūrvamādityenā''tmarūpiṇā
purāṇaṃ kathitaṃ sauraṃ tanno vaktumihārhasi
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanātsākṣātpūrve hi viditaṃ tvayā
tvatto nāsti paro vaktā purāṇānāṃ mahātapaḥ
santyanye bahavaḥ śiṣyā api tasya mahātmanaḥ
tathā'pei śiṣyavātsalyāttvaṃ purāṇeṣu yojitaḥ
yānyanyāni purāṇāni tvayoktāni mahāmune
śivabhaktimṛte yasmānmuktirnāstīti śuśruma
devo'yaṃ bhagavānbhānurantaryāmī sanātanaḥ
yo brūte sarvavastūnāṃ tattvaṃ jñātvaiva nānyathā
ataḥ śraddhā hi mahatī śrotuṃ tvadvadanāmṛtam
asmākaṃ vartate sūtaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata
sūta uvāca
natvā sūrya paraṃ dhāma ṛgyajuḥ sāmarūpiṇam
purāṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sauraṃ śivakathāśrayam
yacchrutvā manujaḥ śīghraṃ pāpakañcukamutsṛjet
paurāṇī vṛttimāśritya ye jīvanti dvijātayaḥ
māhātmyaṃ kathyate śaṃbharnāstyasmādadhikaṃ dvijāḥ
idaṃ purāṇaṃ vaktavyaṃ dhārmikāyānasūyave
dhānāya śivaikātibuddhaye
āsīnmanuḥ sūryasuto vartate yo mahātapāḥ
sa kadācinmahābhāgaḥ kāmikākhyaṃ vanaṃ yayau
tattvaṃ vicārayāmāsurmitho yatra maharṣayaḥ
aśaktāste mahābhāgā bhṛgvādyāstattvanirṇaye
evaṃ sthiteṣu vipreṣu māyayā mohitātmasu
saṃśayāviṣṭacitteṣu vāgabhūdaśarīriṇī
śrutvā tu munayaḥ sarve bhṛgvādyā dagdhakilviṣāḥ
mainuṃ puraskṛtya yayuḥ kṣetraṃ vai dvādaśātmanaḥ
viśrutaṃ dvādaśādityamiti lokeṣu tadvijāḥ
paśyantu māṃ paraṃ devaṃ viśvāntaryāmiṇaṃ vibhum
sūta uvāca
iti dṛṣṭvā raviṃ sākṣātpratyakṣaṃ purataḥ sthitam
mene kṛtārthamātmānaṃ manurvaivasvatastadā
ātmanyātmānamādhāya sarvabhāvena saṃyamī
nama namo vareṇyāya varadāyāṃśumāline
trilokacakṣuṣe tubhyaṃ triguṇāyāmṛtāya ca
naranārīśarīrāya namo mīdṛṣṭamāya te
majñānāyākhileśāya saptāśvāya trimūrtaye
namo vyāhṛtirūpāya trilakṣāyā''śugāmine
ekalakṣavilakṣāya bahulakṣāya daṇḍine
ekasaṃsthādvisaṃsthāya bahusaṃsthāya te namaḥ
śaktitrayāya śuklāya ravaye parameṣṭhine
tvaṃ śivatvaṃ harirdeva tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ divaspatiḥ
tvamakāro vaṣaṭkāraḥ svadhā svāhā tvameva hi
tvāmṛte paramātmānaṃ na tatpaśyāmi daivatam
munibhiḥ saha dharmātmā samyagdarśanakāṅkṣibhiḥ
jñāte tasmiṃstu kiṃ rūpaṃ tasya jñānaṃ kimātmakam
caritaṃ tasya kiṃ tāta kiṃ tīrthaṃ tadadhiṣṭhitam
lakṣaṇaṃ ca purāṇānāṃ vratānāṃ ca kramo yathā
varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca varṇācāravidhiḥ katham
śrāddhaṃ kathaṃ vā kriyate prāyaścittavidhiḥ katham
etatsarvaṃ hi bhagavanpṛṣṭaṃ vaktumihārhasi
evaṃ manorvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānbhāskaro dvijāḥ
yatpṛṣṭaṃ tadaśeṣeṇa vaktuṃ samupacakrame
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde naimiṣāraṇya praśaṃsādikathanaṃ nāma prathamo'dhyāyaḥ
bhānuruvāca
śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi tattvaṃ yatra pratiṣṭhitam
purāṇe'sminmahābhāga sarvavedārthasaṃgrahe
tattvaṃ yadbhagavato rūpamīśasya śūlinaḥ
viśvaṃ tenākhilaṃ vyāptaṃ nānyenetyabravīcchrutiḥ
sa evā''tmā samastānāṃ bhūtānāṃ manujādhipa
caitanyarūpī bhagavānmahādevaḥ sahomayā
masti bahudhā bhāti līlayā kevalaḥ śivaḥ
brahmaviṣṇvādirūpeṇa devadevo maheśvaraḥ
pṛṣṭo brahmādibhirdevaiḥ kastvaṃ deveti śaṃkaraḥ
abravīdahamevaiko nānyaḥ kaściditi śrutiḥ
ātmabhūtānmahādevāllīlāvigraharūpiṇaḥ
tamekaṃ paramātmānamādi kartāramīśvaram
prāhurbahuvidhaṃ tajjñā indraṃ mitramiti śrutiḥ
na tasmādadhikaḥ kaścinnāṇīyānapi kaścana
tenedamakhilaṃ pūrṇa śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā
mumukṣubhiḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ śiva eko nirañjanaḥ
ānandarūpayā gauryā krīḍati sma maheśvaraḥ
akṣeraṃ paramaṃ vyoma śaivaṃ jyotiranāmayam
nānyo vedyaḥ svayaṃjyotī rudra eko nirañjanaḥ
tasmijjñāte'khilaṃ jñātamityāhurvedavādinaḥ
ahaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuśva śakraścānye divaukasaḥ
adyāpyupāyairvividhaiḥ śaṃbhodarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
bhaktyaivānanyayā rājañjñāyate bhagavāśivaḥ
bhargādviśvasya bharaṇādviśvayonerumāpateḥ
tasya jñānamayī śaktiravyayā girijā śivā
ācakṣate tayorbhedamajñā na paramārthataḥ
māyā sā paramā śaktirakṣairā girijā'vyayā
māyāviśvātmako rudraratajjñātvā hyamṛtī bhavet
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ prāyaṇe kāraṇaṃ param
śivabhaktiḥ sadā satyaṃ nānyakiṃcana bhūtale
trilokyāṃ sukhakāmo yastena pūjyaḥ sadāśivaḥ
śivabhaktiḥ mṛte saukhyaṃ kutaḥ syāt dehinām
śivabhaktyā dhanaṃ vidyā yaśaḥ śatranayastathā
yadā lalāṭe sukhaprāptirlikhitā bhavetsadā śivasevāyāṃ matirbhavatīti vedasiddhāntaḥ
svātmanyavasthitaṃ devaṃ viśvavyāpinamīśvaram
bhaktyā paramayā rājañjñātvā pāśairvimucyate
saṃkalaṃ tasya bhāsaiva bhāti nānyena śaṃkaraḥ
tasminprakāśamāne hi naiva bhāntyanalādayaḥ
tasminmaheśvare gūḍhe vidyāvidye kṣarākṣare
vidhātari jagannāthe viśvaṃ bhāti na vastutaḥ
tasmiñjñāte'khilaiḥ pāśairmucyate manujeśvaraḥ
sarve krīḍanakāstasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ
ādisarge mahādevo brahmāṇamasṛjatprabhuḥ
dakṣiṇāṅgādvirūpākṣaḥ sṛṣṭyarthe līlayā kila
asṛjatpālanārthaṃ ca vāmabhāgānmaheśvaraḥ
hṛdayātkāla rudrākhyaṃ jagasaṃhārakārakam
asṛjadyogināṃ dhyeyo nirguṇastu svayaṃ śivaḥ
viśvaṃ tasmāddhi saṃbhūtaṃ tasmistiṣṭhati śaṃkare
sa evā''tmā mahādevaḥ sarveṣāmeva dehinām
jñānene bhaktiyuktena jñātavyaḥ parameśvaraḥ
na paśyāmi mahādevādadhikaṃ devatāntaram
vedā api tamevārthamāhuḥ svāyaṃbhuve'ntare
vedā ūcuyaṃ prapaśyanti vidvāṃso yoginaḥ kṣapitāśayāḥ
niyamya karaṇagrāmaṃ sa evā''tmā maheśvaraḥ
yasya prasādājjīvanti sa devaḥ pārvatīpatiḥ
na jānanti paraṃ bhāvaṃ yasya brahmādayaḥ surāḥ
śṛṇvantu devatāḥ sarvāḥ satyamasmadvacaḥ param
nāsti rudrānmahādevādadhikaṃ daivataṃ param
na yathā kūrmaromāṇi śṛṅgaṃ na śaśamastake
mahādevaṃ vijānīyādehamasmīti paṇḍitaḥ
brāhmī nārāyaṇī raudrī pūjayitvā maheśvarīm
yatprapaśyanti yogīndrāttadvidyācchāṃkaraṃ padam
kramāccatrāṇi caṃkramya śaṅkhinyāmupari sthitam
devayānapathaṃ hitvā pitṛyāṇaṃ tathottaram
gaganādyo ravaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śaṃkarasya sa vācakaḥ
viśvataścakṣurīśānatriśūlī viśvatomukhaḥ
janakaḥ sarvabhūtānāmeka eva maheśvaraḥ
vālāgramātraṃ hṛtpadme sthitaṃ devamumāpatim
ye'nupaśyanti vidvāṃsara teṣāṃ śāntirhi śāśvatī
pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhati vibhuḥ pṛthivī vetti naiva tam
rūpaṃ ca pṛthivī yasya tasmai bhūmyātmane namaḥ
yosar tiṣṭhatyameyātmā na taṃ vetti kadācana
sūrye tiṣṭhati yo devo na sūryo vetti śaṃkaram
yaścandre tiṣṭhati virbhuścandro vetti na śāśvatam
yajamāno'pi yadrūpaṃ yajamānātmane namaḥ
pramāṇapadamārūḍhāstvatprasādādvṛṣadhvaja
bhānuruvāca
evaṃ vedastutiṃ śrutvā bhagavāngirijāpatiḥ
pratyakṣaḥ samabhūtteṣāṃ vedānāṃ manujādhipa
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sūrya somāgnilocanaḥ
sthūlātsthūlataraḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraḥ paraḥ
īśvara uvāca
matprasādādbhaviṣyadhvaṃ he vedā lokapūjitāḥ
yuṣmānāśritya viprendrāḥ karma kurvanti nānyathā
niṣphalaṃ tadbhavetkarma teṣāṃ yuṣmadaivajñayā
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ yaccānyanmokṣasādhanam
ye vai yuṣmānanādṛtya śāstraṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ
yuṣmatkṛtaṃ paraṃ stotraṃ ye paṭhiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ
teṣāmadhyayanaṃ puṇyaṃ matprasādādbhaviṣyati
bhānuruvāca
akṣaraṃ nirguṇaṃ śuddhamānandaṃ paramavyayam
pratyakṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāmajñānāṃ tadviparyayaḥ
viśvamāyāvidhātāraṃ diraṣṭādaśarūpaṇam
bhaktigrādyaṃ mahādevaṃ jānīyātmani saṃsthitam
bhaktimāsthāya paramoṃ paraṃ nirvāṇamāpnuhi
tīrthayātrā bahuvidhā yajñāśca vividhāḥ kṛtāḥ
yeṣāṃ janmasahasreṣu teṣāṃ bhaktirbhavecchive
tatrākṣayaḥ paro dharmaḥ śivadharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
yajñāttīrthājjapādānāddharmaḥ syādbahusādhanaḥ
sādhanaprārthanākleśaḥ parasaṃpattiduḥkhadaḥ
saṃcitaṃ janmasāhasraiḥ pāpaṃ rūpamaṃ yadi
te vijñeyā mahātmāna iti satyaṃ bravīmyaham
pādmakalpa samudbhūtāṃ brahmaṇā samudīritām
'śraddhayā parayā rājañśṛṇu tvaṃ gadato mama
vakṣye'haṃ taṃ praṇamyāssdāvīśaṃ bhuvananāyakam
āsīdādye kṛtayuge saptadvīpaikarāvalī
pratiṣṭhānapure ramye gaṅgātīre manorame
tatra sthitvā'khilāṃ pṛthvīṃ tasminrājani śāsati
kadācittatra bhagavāṃstṛṇabindurmahāmuniḥ
ājagāma sa taṃ draṃ sudyumnaṃ priyadarśanam
tamāyāntaṃ muniṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā rudrārcane rataḥ
udvāsyāca mahābāhurutthāya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ
bhagavānāgato yasmānmāṃ draṣṭuṃ munisattama
bhānuruvāca
sudyumnasya vacaḥ śrutvā munirāha mahāmanāḥ
tṛṇabinduruvāca
tathāpi caritaṃ śrutvā tavāhaṃ vismayānvitaḥ
kathayasva mahābāho śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
jānāti bhagavāneko viśvavyāpī maheśvaraḥ
idaṃ puṇyamiti jñātvā kṛtaṃ nānena yadyapi
āhara praharetyādi nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ ca yat
karoti tena puṇyena duṣkṛtaṃ bhasmasātkṛtam
pāpaleśo'pi nāsyāsti iti me niścitā matiḥ
suvyāḍiṃ pūjayāmāsa yathāvadvidhipūrvakam
sūryātapratīkāśaṃ divya strībhirvirājitam
devadūtaiḥ samānītamāruhya munipuṃgava
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānyugānāmayutaṃ tataḥ
tatastu karmaṇaḥ śeṣaṃ bhoktumatra mahītale
smarāmi pūrvikāṃ jātiṃ prasādācchūlino mune
jānāti ko maheśasya māhātmyaṃ paramātmanaḥ
yasya nāmnaḥ phalamidamajñānoccāraṇādapi
jñātvā yaḥ kīrtayecchaṃ bhornāmānyamitatejasaḥ
bhānuruvāca
iti sarvamaśeṣeṇa caritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
sunasya muniḥ śrutvā vismito'bhūtpunaḥ punaḥ
samāliṅganya mahātmānaṃ sunaṃ rājapuṃgavam
rājasvamāśramapadaṃ yāmītyuktvā jagāma saḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure bhānumanusaṃvāde sudyunnākhyānaṃ nāma tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ
rājñaḥ sakāśātsa munirmatvā kiṃ kṛtavānpunaḥ
bhānuruvāca
revātīre mahatpuṇyaṃ jāleśvaramiti smṛtam
āśramaṃ tṛṇavindastu muni siddhaniṣevitam
śivaliṅga pratiṣṭhāpya tīrthayātrāṃ cakāra saḥ
kāni tīrthāni guhyāni yeṣu saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ
bhānuruvāca
tīrthānāmuttamaṃ tīrthaṃ kṣetrāṇāṃ kṣetramuttamam
vārāṇasītinagarī priyā devasya śulinaḥ
yaṃtra viśveśvaro devaḥ sarveṣāmiha dehinām
dadāti tārakaṃ jñānaṃ saṃsārānmocakaṃ param
gaṅgā brahmamayī yatra mūrtiścottarabāhinī
saṃhatra sarvapāpānāṃ dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā namaskṛtā
nāsti gaṅgāsamaṃ tīrthe vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
kiṃ tacchreyaskaramiti hṛdi kṛtvā jagāma saḥ
nandīśvarasya yaḥ śiṣyo yogināmagraṇīḥ svayam
jānādevagaṇākīrṇe yakṣagandharvasevite
siddhacāraṇakūṣmāṇḍairapsarobhiśca saṃkule
gaṅgā mandākinī yatra rājate duḥkhahāriṇī
tasyā''śramamanuprāpya pārāśaryo mahāmuniḥ
abhivādya yathānyāyaṃ tasyāgra upaviśya ca
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā vākyametaduvāca ha
vyāsa uvāca
prāptaṃ kaliyugaṃ ghoraṃ puṇyamārgabahiṣkṛtam
pākhaṇḍācāranirataṃ mlecchāntrajana saṃkulam
adhārmikāḥ krūraisattvā dhanācīrālpamedhasaḥ
tasminyuge bhaviṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ śūdrayājakāḥ
snānaṃ devārcanaṃ dānaṃ homaṃ ca pitṛtarpaṇam
svādhyāyaṃ na kariṣyanti brāhmaṇā hi kalau yuge
na paṭhanti tathā vedāñśreyase brāhmaṇādhamāḥ
pratigrahārthaṃ vedāṃśca paṭhiṣyanti kalau yuge
puruṣottamamāśritya śivanindāratā dvijāḥ
kalau yuge bhaviṣyanti teṣāṃ trātā na mādhavaḥ
svāṃ svāṃ vṛttiṃ parityajya paravṛttyupajīvakāḥ
brāhmaṇādyā bhaviṣyanti saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge
etānpāparatāndṛṣṭvā rājānaśvāvicārakāḥ
bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte vṛthā jātyabhimāninaḥ
uccāsanagatāḥ śūdrā dṛṣṭvā ca brāhmaṇāṃstadā
kāṣāyaṇaśca nirgranthā nagnāḥ kāpālikāstathā
tapoyajñaphalānāṃ tu vikretāro dvijādhamāḥ
yatayaśca bhaviṣyanti śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ
vinindanti mahādevaṃ saṃsārānmocakaṃ param
tadbhaktāṃśca mahātmano brāhmaṇāṃśca kalau yuge
tāḍayanti durātmāno brāhmaṇānrājasevakāḥ
na nivārayate rājā tāndṛṣṭvā'pi kalau yuge
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure bhānumanusaṃbāde vārāṇasī mahimakaliyugavarṇanaṃ nāma caturtho'dhyāyaḥ
gaccha vārāṇasīṃ vyāsa yatra viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ
viśveśvarasya yalliṅgaṃ jyotirliṃṅgaṃ taducyate
yasmindṛṣṭe kṣaṇājjantuḥ saṃsāraṃ na punarviśet
gatvā paiśya paraṃ liṅgaṃ tatra satyavatīsuta
snātvā gaṅgājale puṇye paśya viśveśvaraṃ param
sa dāsyati paraṃ jñānaṃ yena mukto bhaviṣyasi
dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaraṃ devaṃ yāvattiṣṭhati tsthāsyasi tatkṣaṇāt
āgamiṣyanti munayastvāṃ draṣṭuṃ sarva eva te
brūhi madvacanātteṣāṃ jñānaṃ māheśvaraṃ param
evaṃ satyavatīsūnustanmāhātmyamaśeṣataḥ
sanatkumārātsvaguroḥ śrutvā māheśvarāgraṇīḥ
saśiṣyaḥ prayayau śīghraṃ vyāso vārāṇasīṃ prati
gatvā vārāṇasīṃ vyāsaḥ siddharṣimunisevitām
bhānuruvāca
saṃprāpya kāśīṃ dharmātmā kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ
snātvā yathāvajjāhnavyāṃ tarpayitvā surānpitan
yayau viśveśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ jyotirliṅganmanāmayam
saṃpūjya sarvabhāvena daṇḍavatpraṇipatya ca
devasya dakṣiṇā mūrtāvupaviśya mahāmuniḥ
paśyanviśveśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ jaipanvai śatarudriyam
kṣaṇālliṅgātparaṃ jyotirāvirbhūtaṃ nirañjanam
sūkṣmātsūkṣmaṃ ca paramamānandaṃ tamasaḥ param
yattanmāheśvaraṃ jyotirvedānteṣu pratiṣṭhitam
darśanāttasya ca muneḥ pārāśaryasya dhīmataḥ
divyaṃ māheśvaraṃ jñānamudbhūtaṃ kevalaṃ śivam
advayaṃ nirguṇaṃ śāntaṃ jīvanmuktastadā muniḥ
yasmindṛṣṭe kṣaṇājjñānamuditaṃ mama nirmalam
namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ viśvanāthāya śūline
durvijñeyāprameyāya paramānandarūpiṇe
bhaktipriyāya sūkṣmāya pārvatīśāya te namaḥ
jānāti
viśveśa tattvato mādṛśo janaḥ
vedā api na jānanti sāṅgopaniṣadakramāḥ
bhānuruvāca
śūlapāṇirameyātmā prādurāsīdvṛṣadhvajaḥ
tatastamabravīdvākyaṃ kāruṇyācchubhayā girā
vyāsa uvāca
bhagavankṛtakṛtyo'smi darśanāttava śaṃkara
jātaṃ tvadviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ devānāmapi durlabham
dehi me devadeveśa nānyadiṣṭaṃ varaṃ mama
bhānuruvāca
varaṃ dattvā munīndrāya kṣaṇādantarhito'bhavat
tasmāṭhyāsātparo nānyaḥ śivabhakto jagāye
kṛṣṇo vā devakīsūnurarjuno vā mahāmatiḥ
evaṃ harāllabdhavaraḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
taṃtra yāni ca liṅgāni tāni draṣṭuṃ yayau muniḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure bhānuganusaṃvāde mahādeva varadānaṃ nāma pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcu
kāni divyāni liṅgāni yāni draṣṭuṃ yayau muniḥ
ācakṣva tāni naḥ sūta māhātmyaṃ cāpi kṛtsnaśaḥ
sūta uvāca
yaduktaṃ bhānunā pūrva manave munisattamāḥ
tadeva kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama
āgneyyāmavimuktasya vāpī trailokyaviśrutā
yatra saṃnihitā davo nityaṃ viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ
yaṃtra snānaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā devānāmapi durlabham
teṣāṃ liṅgāni jāyante hṛdaye trīṇi suvratāḥ
tatra satyavatīsūnuḥ khātvā caiva yathāvidhi
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā lāṅgalīśaṃ tato yayau
tatra brahmādayo devāḥ sevante śūlapāṇinam
tasya darśanamātreṇa jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ bhavet
jagāma sa muniḥ paśvādraṣṭuṃ vai tārakeśvaram
yatrāntakāle bhagavāñjñānaṃ tatsaṃprayacchati
taddṛṣṭvā paramaṃ liṅgaṃ vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ
yayau śukreśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam
ārādhya muninā yatra śukreṇāmitatejasā
prāptā saṃjīvanī vidyā surāṇāmapi durlabhā
tasminkūpe muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā śukreśvaraṃ śivam
brahmeśvaraṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ tatra brahmā virāṭ svayam
tapastaptvā mahāghoraṃ prītaye pārvatīpateḥ
brahmatvaṃ prāptavānbrahmā yogaṃ cānye maharṣayaḥ
yatra sākṣācchivaḥ sūkṣmo nityaṃ tiṣṭhati vai dvijāḥ
anugrahāya lokānāṃ paśupāśavimocakaḥ
yatra pāśupatāḥ siddhā oṃkāreśvaramīśvaram
saṃpūjya paramāṃ siddhiṃ prāsavanto dvijottamāḥ
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ tasmiliṅa upoṣitaḥ
yadi jāgaraṇaṃ kuryātparaṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt
tataḥ satyavatīsūnuḥ kṛttivāseśvaraṃ yayau
upāsate mahādevaṃ yatra brahmādayaḥ surāḥ
munayaḥ śaṃsitātmāno rudrajāpyaparāyaṇāḥ
kṛttivāseśvare liṅga līlā nā śca bahavo dvijāḥ
snātvā tatra mahādevaṃ kṛttivāseśvaraṃ śivam
sakṛtpaśyati yo bhaktyā kṛttivāseśvaraṃ vibhum
haṃsatīrthe naraḥ snātvā kṛttivāseśvaraṃ vibhum
saṃpūjya parayā bhaktyā kṛttivāseśvaraṃ śivam
na patatyeva saṃsāre nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
yayau ratneśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ mokṣo yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ
yo'yaṃ pāśupato yogaḥ paśupāśavimocakaḥ
varṣerdvādaśabhiḥ samyakkṛte pāśupate dvijāḥ
ratneśvaraṃ tu saṃpūjya pārāśaryo mahāmuniḥ
draṣṭuṃ devādhideveśaṃ vṛddhakāleśvaraṃ yayau
tasmĩlliṅga mahādevaḥ sadā tiṣṭhati līlayā
anugrahāya lokānāmayā saha viśvabhuk
pṛthivyāṃ yāni liṅgāni santi divyāni vai dvijāḥ
vṛddhakāleśvare dṛṣṭe dṛṣṭānyeva na saṃśayaḥ
devasya pūrvadigbhāge kūpoṃ muniniṣevitaḥ
pūritaḥ puṇyasalilairdevadevena śaṃbhunā
yaiḥ pītaṃ tasya salilaṃ prākṛtaiśculukatrayam
tatra dvaipāyano viprāḥ snānaṃ kṛtvā samāhitaḥ
buddhakāleśvara liṅgaṃ saṃpūjya ca tato yayau
madhyameśvaranāmānaṃ mokṣaliṅgamanuttamam
upāsate paraṃ liṅgaṃ śivadarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
mandākinyāṃ muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai madhyameśvaram
ghaṇṭākarṇa snātvā liṅga tadvimalaṃ śivam
pratiṣṭhāpya muniśreṣṭho labdhavāñjñānamuttamam
satra dṛṣṭvā vyāseśvaraṃ śivam
yatra yatra mṛto vā'pi vārāṇasyāṃ mṛto bhavet
tataḥ satyavatīsūnuḥ kapardīśvaramīśvaram
draṣṭuṃ jagāma dipendrā liṅgaṃ tatpārameśvaram
ye drakṣyanti kapardīśaṃ kṛtārthāste na saṃśayaḥ
mānuṣīṃ tanumāśritya rudrā eva na saṃśayaḥ
tasmiṃstīrthe muniḥ snātvā saṃtarpya ca surānpitṝn
kapardīśvaramīśānaṃ saṃpūjya prayayau muniḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde vārāṇasī liṅgapahimavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
punarjagāma bhagavānkṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
dra dakṣeśvaraṃ devaṃ bhaktānāṃ siddhidāyakam
yacchivāvajñayā pāpaṃ jātaṃ dakṣaprajāpateḥ
tasya pāpasya mokṣāya tasmĩlliṅge dvijottamāḥ
ārādhya devadeveśaṃ bahūnyabdaśatāni vai
vairaṃ nidhāya manasi śaṃbhunā saha suvratāḥ
dakṣaḥ prācetaso yajñamakarojjāhnavītaṭe
tasminyajñe samāhūtā indrādyā devatāgaṇāḥ
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhā rājānaḥ prathitaujasaḥ
brahmā ca viṣṇunā sārdhamāhūtastena dhīmatā
devānsarvāṃśca bhāgārthamahūtānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
dṛṣṭvā śivena rahitāndakṣaṃ pratyevamabravīt
aho dakṣa mahāmūṃḍha durbuddhe kiṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā
devāḥ sarve samāhūtāḥ śaṃkareṇa vinā katham
antaryāmī sa viśveśaḥ sarveṣāmeva dehinām
bhoktā sa sarvayajñānāṃ śaṃkaraḥ paramārthataḥ
ete ca munayaḥ sarve tava sāhāyyakāriṇaḥ
na jānanti paraṃ bhāvaṃ mahādevasya śūlinaḥ
ete ca devāḥ śakrādyā āgatā yajñabhāginaḥ
tanmāyāmohitāḥ sarve na jānanti pinākinam
yasya pādarajaḥsparśādbrahmatvaṃ prāptavānaham
dharmādharmavyavasthā ca varṇāścaivā''śramaṇi ca
tiṣṭhanti śāsanāttasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ
sā ca śaktiḥ parā gaurī svecchāvigrahacāriṇī
kastāṃ jānāti viśveśīmīśvarārdhaśarīriṇīm
ahaṃ nādyāpi jānāmi cakrī śakrasya kā kathā
svecchāvigraharūpiṇyā gauryā saha pinākadhṛt
bhrāmayatyakhilaṃ viśvamiti satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
sa eva badhnāti paśūnasmadādīnmaheśvaraḥ
sa eva mocako devaḥ paśūnāṃ na iti śrutiḥ
nāmasaṃkīrtanādyasya bhidyate pāpañjaram
śaṃbhoravajñā yatrāssste sthātavyaṃ naiva sūribhiḥ
sūta uvāca
dadhīcirabravīdakṣaṃ munīnāmagraṇīḥ svayam
dadhīciruvāca
kathaṃ devādhideveśaḥ karmasākṣī sanātanaḥ
viśveśvaro mahādevastvayā dakṣa na pūjyate
vācakaḥ praṇavo yasya jñānamūrterumāpateḥ
anugrahaṃ vinā tasya kathaṃ jānāti śūlinam
prasaṅgātkautukāllobhādbhayādajñānato'pi vā
aho dakṣa tavājñānaṃ tava nāśasya kāraṇam
evaṃ dadhīcervacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo vicakṣaṇaḥ
dadhīcimabravīdviprāḥ śakrādīnāṃ ca saṃnidhau
dakṣa uvāca
nāhaṃ nārāyaṇāddevātpaśyāmyanyaṃ dvijottama
kāraṇaṃ sarvavastūnāṃ nāstītyaiva suniścitam
dadhīciruvāca
sa eva kāraṇaṃ nānyo viṣṇorapi hi vai śrutiḥ
yajñasya pālako viṣṇuriti yanniścitaṃ tvayā
bhaviṣyatyanyathaivā''śu paśyataḥ kamalāpateḥ
ete ca brāhmaṇāḥ sarve ye dviṣainti maheśvaram
pāpaṇḍācāraniratāḥ sarve nirayagāminaḥ
kalau yuge tu saṃprāpte daridrāḥ śūdrayājakāḥ
sarvasmādadhiko rudraḥ paśupāśavimocakaḥ
parāṅmukhastu yuṣmākaṃ mā dijyākarī gatiḥ
svāśramaṃ munibhirjuṣṭamoṃkāraṃ narmadātaṭe
dakṣayajñasya vṛttāntaṃ śrutvā devaṛṣermukhāt
māha viśvādhikaṃ rudraṃ mãṇatārtiprabhañjanam
nirīkṣyamāṇaṃ deveśī parānandaikavigraham
śrīdevyuvāca
yo'yaṃ prācetaso dakṣaḥ pitā me pūrvajanmani
āvāmavajñāya kathaṃ yajñaṃ kartuṃ pracakrame
devāḥ sarve samāhūtā viṣṇunā saha śaṃkara
ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyāścaiva marudraṇāḥ
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhā daiteyā dānavāśca ye
rājānaśca mahābhāgā gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāstathā
avajñākāriṇastasya yajñaṃ śīghraṃ vināśaya
evaṃ devyā vacaḥ śrutvā devadevaḥ pinākadhṛt
asṛjattatkṣaṇācchaṃbhuvīrabhadraṃ mahābalam
sahasrabāhuṃ jaṭilaṃ duṣṭānāṃ ca bhayaṃkaram
bhaktānāṃ varadaṃ devaṃ sūryasomāgnilocanam
umākopodbhavā devī bhadrakālī bhayaṃkarī
anyāśca devyo rudrāśca śataśo romasaṃbhavaḥ
bhadrakālyā saha tadā vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ
gatvā sa yajñaṃ dakṣasya bhasmasādakarodvijāḥ
dakṣastadadbhutaṃ karma dṛṣṭvā'tha bhayavihvalaḥ
gatastaccharaṇaṃ śīghraṃ vīrabhadrasya śūlinaḥ
uvāca vīrabhadrastaṃ dakṣaṃ prācetasaṃ dvijāḥ
tasya pāpavimokṣāya kāruṇyāmṛtavāridhiḥ
gaccha vārāṇasīṃ dakṣa sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ
anenaiva śarīreṇa tatra mokṣaṃ gamiṣyasi
sūta uvāca
vīrabhadrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo mahāmatiḥ
gatvā vārāṇasīṃ śīghraṃ sarvasaṅgavivarjitaḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya mahāliṅga gaṅgātīre manorame
ārādhya parayā bhaktyā tasmĩlliṅge layaṃ gataḥ
dakṣeśvarasya māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
trilocanasya māhātmyaṃ sāṃprataṃ varṇyate mayā
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrī saure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde dakṣeśvara māhātmyādikathanaṃ nāma saptamo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
trilocanātparaṃ liṅgaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ na dṛśyate
yāni sthitāni liṅgāni vārāṇasyāṃ dvijottamāḥ
dṛṣṭānyeva bhavantyeva dṛṣṭe liṅga trilocane
asaṃkhyātāni pāpāni jñānato'jñānato'pi vā
kṛtāni nāśayatyevaṃ devadevastrilocanaḥ
māyāpāśena baddhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināmapi
paścimābhimukhaṃ liṅgaṃ sarpamekhalamaṇḍitam
tasya darśanamātreṇa koṭiliṅgārcanaṃ phalam
trilocanaṃ susaṃpūjya kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ
yayau kāmeśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ siddhaliṅgamanuttamam
prasanno vividhāḥ siddhīḥ sarveṣāmapi durlabhāḥ
kṛtānāṃ kriyamāṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ tapasāmapi
tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge kāmakuṇḍamiti smṛtam
tatra snātvā naro bhaktyā dṛṣṭvā kāmeśvaraṃ śivam
anyānyapi ca liṅgāni vārāṇasyāṃ sthitānyapi
saṃkhyāmapi na jānāti teṣāṃ devavaturmukhaḥ
ko vā vadati māhātmyamṛte devānmaheśvarāt
nandīśvaro vā jānāti prasādāgirijāpateḥ
atha satyavatīsūnudraṣṭuṃ devīṃ śivāṃ parām
viśālākṣī dvijaśreṣṭhā yatra saṃnihitā śivā
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vidhivadbhaktyā saṃpūjya ca mahāmuniḥ
parīnandātmikāṃ gaurīṃ stutiṃ matvā cakāra saḥ
vyāsa uvāca
viśālākṣi namastubhyaṃ parabrahmātmake śive
tvameva mātā sarveṣāṃ brahmādīnāṃ divaukasām
ṛjvī kuṇḍalinī sukṣmā yogasiddhipradāyinī
svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā meghā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī
satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā sarvaśaktimayī śivā
aparṇā caikaparṇā ca tathā caikaikapāṭalā
umā haimavatī cāpi kalyāṇī caitra mātṛkā
khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurīti viśrutā
gaṇāmbikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī
sāvitrī varadā puṇyā pāvanī lokaviśrutā
āryatī niyatī raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī
kālarātrī mahāmāyā revatī bhūtanāyikā
gautamī kauśikī cāssrthā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī
vṛṣadhvajā śūladharā paramā brahmacāriṇī
mahendropendramātā ca pārvatī siṃhavāhanā
evaṃ stutvā viśālākṣī divyaistaiḥ sunāmabhiḥ
kṛtakṛtyo'bhavadvyāso vārāṇasyāṃ dvijottamāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃ viśālākṣī gaṅgā viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ
yaḥ paśyati viśālākṣīṃ snātvā gaṅgāmbhasi dvijāḥ
vārāṇasyāstu māhātmyamiti kiṃcinmayoditam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvā'pi yāti māheśvaraṃ padam
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde trilocana māhātmyādikathanaṃ namāmo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kiṃ lakṣaṇaṃ purāṇānāṃ teṣāṃ dānena kiṃ phalam
anyeṣāmapi dānānāṃ vratānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca teṣāṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ yathā
tataḥ śrāddhavidhānaṃ ca prāyaścittaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍaṃ proktaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ ca tataḥ param
bhāgadvayena kathitaṃ brahmāṇḍamati saṃjñitam
khilānyupapurāṇāni yāni coktāni sūribhiḥ
saṃhitādvayasaṃyuktaṃ puṇyaṃ śivakathāśrayam
āyā sanatkumāroktā dvitīyā sūryabhāṣitā
iyaṃ puṇyatamā khyātā saṃhitā pāpanāśinī
dānamasya purāṇasya dānānāmuttamaṃ dvijāḥ
yāni dānāni lokeṣu prasiddhāni dvijottamāḥ
sarveṣāṃ phalamāpnoti caturdaśyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
brāhmaṃ purāṇaṃ prathamaṃ dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇumuddiśya dvādaśyāṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ
anūcānāya yo dadyādvaiṣṇavaṃ padamāpnuyāt
dadāti sūryabhaktāya yastu bhāgavataṃ dvijāḥ
vaiśākhe śuklapakṣasya tṛtīyā'kṣayasaṃjñitā
tasyāṃ tithau saṃyatātmā brāhmaṇāyā''hitāśaye
bhaviṣyākhyaṃ purāṇaṃ tu dadāti śraddhayānvitaḥ
markaṇḍeyaṃ tu yo dadyātsaptabhyāṃ prayatātmavān
rājasūyasva yajñasya phalaṃ bhavati śāśvatam
dadāti nāradīyaṃ yaścaturdaśyāṃ samāhitaḥ
kārtikasya caturdaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya suvaitāḥ
laiṅgaṃ dadyādvijendrāya śivārcanaratāya vai
dvādaśyāṃ saṃyato bhūtvā brāhmaṇāya tapasvine
yo vai dadāti vārāhaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati
skāndaṃ śivacaturdaśyāṃ pradadyācchviyogine
jñānī bhavati viprendrā mahādevaprasādataḥ
dvādaśyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ dadyādvāmanamuttamam
mātsyaṃ dadyādvijendrāya prayatīttarāyaṇe
gāruḍaṃ śivamuddiśya dadyācchvitithau dvijāḥ
śivasya purato bhaktyā saṃprāpte dakṣiṇāyane
gaṇādhipatyamānoti devadevasya śūlinaḥ
evamuktaḥ purāṇānāṃ kramo dānena yatphalam
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde brāhmādi purāṇa kramadānaphalakathanaṃ nāma navamo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
dānaṃ pātre pradātavyaṃ nāpātre 'pyaṇumātrakam
pātrabhūtānpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
dānena māpnuyātsaukhyaṃ rūpaṃ kānti yaśo balam
dānena śatrūñjayati vyādhirdānena naśyati
taramādānāya satpātraṃ vicāryaiva prayatnataḥ
vedavedāṅgatatvajñāḥ śāntāścaiva jitendriyāḥ
śrautasmārtakriyāniṣṭhāḥ satyaniṣṭhāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ
tapasvinaratīrthatāḥ kṛtajñā mitabhāṣiṇaḥ
guruśuśrūṣaṇairatā nirtya svādhyāyaśīlinaḥ
mahādevārcanaratā bhūtiśāsanabhūṣitāḥ
vaiṣṇavāḥ sūryabhaktā vā pātrabhūtā dvijottamāḥ
uttamaḥ sarvapātrāṇāṃ taramai dattaṃ tadakṣayam
tasmātpāyatamaṃ jñātvā śivabhaktamakalmaṣam
dānaṃ pāpaviśuddhayarthaṃ śraddhayā yatpradīyate
proktaṃ naimittikaṃ dānamṛṣibhirvedavādibhiḥ
putrārthaṃ vā dhanārtha vā svargārthaṃ vā'nyato'pi vā
dānaṃ tadvimalaṃ proktaṃ kevalaṃ mokṣasādhanam
yatkiṃcidīyate dānaṃ daridrāya viśeṣataḥ
svalpāmapi mahīṃ yastu dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
sa yāti brahmasadanaṃ yatra devaḥ svayaṃ virāṭ
ikṣugodhūmatuvarīyavaiśca sahitāṃ mahīm
api gocarmamātrāṃ yo dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
śivabhaktāya śāntāya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
na bhūmidānādadhikaṃ dānamastīha bhūtale
tavānaṃ hi daridrāya dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam
āḍhayāya naiva dātavyaṃ bhūmidānaṃ viśeṣataḥ
yairdattā brāhmaṇebhyaśca grāmāḥ paramadhārmikaiḥ
gṛhṇanti ye karaṃ teṣu lobhāndhāḥ pāpino nṛpāḥ
tadante makṣikā yūkā matkuṇā maśakāstathā
kṛmayo jālapādārthe śūkarāḥ pakṣiṇastathā
śvāno godhāḥ śaśāḥ sedhā gardabhāśva pipīlikāḥ
mūṣakāḥ kṛkalāsāśca vṛkṣagulmādayastathā
na teṣāṃ niṣkṛtirddaṣṭā prāyaścittaśatairapi
brahmahā śuddhimānoti kālena munipuṅgavāḥ
dvijagrāmakaragrāhī naiva śuddhimavāpnuyāt
vimaidānakarādānādadhikaṃ nāsti pātakam
dānānāmuttamaṃ dānaṃ vidyādānaṃ vidurbudhāḥ
tacca dānaṃ vinītāya varṇāśramaratāya ca
brāhmaṇāyaiva śāntāya śuśrūṣaṇaratāya ca
annadānaṃ praśaṃsanti viduṣo vedavādinaḥ
anameva yataḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇadānasamaṃ hi tat
aparīkṣyaiva sarvebhya iti svāyaṃbhuśāsanāt
mītaśca bhagavāñranenaiva śacīpatiḥ
tasmādviśiṣṭaṃ tadeyamāhurveda vido budhāḥ
nādhvagāya niṣiddhaṃ taditi devo'bravīdraviḥ
jīvanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jalameva dvijottamāḥ
tiladaḥ putramāproti vāsodaḥ kāntimuttamām
dīpadī nirmalāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ yānadaḥ śriyamuttamām
śayyāpradaśvāpi tathā dhānyadaḥ saukhyamuttamam
tena dānena mahatā sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam
gṛhītvā vetanaṃ vedaṃ yo'dhyāpayati mūḍhadhīḥ
adhīte yo hi vā dattvā tāvubhau pāpinī smṛtau
surābhāṇḍagataṃ toyaṃ yathā bhavati ninditam
gavāṃ grāsapradānena mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
yāni bhojyāni mūlāni phalāni vividhāni ca
śākāni brāhmaṇebhyaśca dattvā'tyantaṃ sukhī bhavet
indhanānāṃ pradānena jāṭharāgnipradīpanam
rogahīnaḥ sa dīrghāyuḥ sukhī bhavati sarvadā
gāmalaṃkṛtya yo dadyātsavatsāṃ ca sadakṣiṇām
ṣoḍaśa ṛtavo ye ca dānaṃ tīrtheṣu yatsmṛtam
tadakṣayaṃ bhaveddānaṃ yogine ca viśeṣataḥ
saṃkrāntyādiṣu kāleṣu dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam
śivamuddiśya yaddattaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu
śivālaye viśeṣeṇa dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam
viśākharkṣeṇa saṃyuktā vaiśākhī pūrṇimā bhavet
tasyāṃ tithau tu saṃpūjya brāhmaṇānsapta pañca vā
kṛṣṇaireva tilairvidvānmadhuna vā'pyupoṣitaḥ
dharmarājo yamaḥ sākṣātmīyatāmiti śaktitaḥ
yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikairvā manogataiḥ
mucyate tatkṣaṇādeva dharmarājaprasādataḥ
kṛṣṇājine tilānkṛtvā hiraṇyaṃ madhusarpiṣī
gāmannamudakumbhaṃ ca vaiśākhyāṃ saṃprayacchati
masiddhā yā śivatithirmādhe kṛṣṇacaturdaśī
dadāti hema vāso vā phalaṃ dhānyamathāpi vā
abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dadyādānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
paṭhedyaḥ śṛṇuyādvā'pi godānasya phalaṃ labhet
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsore sūtaśonakasaṃvāde dānāha vimādikathanaṃ nāma daśamo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
anyadvratamidaṃ vakṣye śṛṇudhvaṃ sunieṅgavāḥ
śivena kathitaṃ sākṣātsvayaṃ skandāya pṛcchate
devadeva mahādeva śaśāṅkakṛtaśekhara
bharga viśveśvareśāna kāruṇyāmṛtavāridhe
kasya prasīdati kṣipraṃ kena vā jñāyate bhavān
yogastvadviṣayaḥ ko vā jñānaṃ tvadvipayaṃ ca kimūḥ
īśvara uvāca
sarvāśī sarvabhakṣī vā sarvācāravilopakaḥ
matparo vāmanaḥkāyairmukta eva na saṃśayaḥ
tuṣṭo'haṃ bhaktileśena kṣipraṃ yacche paraṃ padam
tripuṇḍradhārī satataṃ śānto rudrākṣakaṅkaṇaḥ
sūryavahnīndu bhaktānāmuttamo vaiṣṇavaḥ paraḥ
vaiṣṇavānāṃ sahastrebhyaḥ śivabhakto viśiṣyate
yadi pāparataḥ krūraḥ svāśramācāravarjitaḥ
saṃ
yespi dambhaṃ samāśritya bhaktānāmupajīvikāḥ
saṃsārātte'pi mucyante kiṃ punarmatparā janāḥ
madbhaktānāṃ ca māhātmyaṃ ko vā jānāti tattvataḥ
'jāne'haṃ tvaṃ ca jānāsi nandī jānāti vā guha
mārgastho vā'pyamārgastho mūrkho vā praṇḍito'pi vā
sa vaḥ sminpustake caturdaśādhyāyasthāne saṃgṛhītaḥ
advaitamekaṃ parasamātmānaṃ jñānavigraham
paśyanti jñāninastvekamātmarūpamidaṃ jagat
ahamātmā vibhuḥ śuddhaḥ sphaṭikopalasaṃnibhaḥ
upādhirahitaḥ śāntaḥ svayaṃjyotiḥ prakāśakaḥ
ātmanyevākhilaṃ bhāti śuktikārajataṃ yathā
śuktitattvaparijñānāttannāśastadvadātmani
na tena lipyate hyātmā puṇyāpuṇyākhyakarmaṇā
buddhyādayo guṇāḥ sarve bhūdbuddherakṛtiḥ
ahaṃkārācca sūkṣmāṇi tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca
sūkṣmebhyaḥ pañca bhūtāni tebhyaḥ sthūlamidaṃ jagat
caturviṃśakamavyaktaṃ puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ
na tasya kārya karaṇaṃ kriyārūpaṃ ca vidyate
svājñānātkathitaṃ sarvamātmanyeveti ca śrutiḥ
iti madviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ kathitaṃ tava putraka
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde śivabhakta mahimādikathanaṃ nāmaikādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
īśvara uvāca
sādhanānyaṣṭadhā tasya pravakṣyāmyadhunā śṛṇu
yamāśca niyamāstāvadāsanānyapi ṣaṇmukhaṃ
prāṇāyāmastataḥ proktaḥ pratyāhāraśca dhāraṇā
dhyānaṃ tathā samādhiśca yogāṅgāni pracakṣate
māḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktā niyamāñśṛṇu putraka
paḥ svādhyāya saṃtoṣaḥ śaucamīśvarapūjanam
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāmakleśajananaṃ hi yat
thārthakathanaṃ satyamasteyamadhunā śṛṇu
vauryeṇa vā balenāpi parasvaharaṇaṃ ca yaṃ
vyāṇāmapyanādānamāpadyapi yathecchayā
vāndrāyaṇādinā yattu śarīrasya ca śoṣaṇam
uttapaḥ kathitaṃ putra svādhyāyamadhunā śṛṇu
raṇavaḥ śatarudrīyaṃ tathā'tharvaśiraḥ śikhā
eteṣāṃ yo japaḥ putra svādhyāya iti kīrtitaḥ
padṛcchālābhasaṃtuṣṭaḥ saṃtoṣa iti paṭhyate
bāhye cābhyantare cāpi śuddhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate
stutismaraṇapūjābhirvāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ
mayi bhaktirdṛḍhā putra etadīśvarapūjanam
yamāśca niyamāḥ proktāḥ saṃkṣepānna tu vistarāt
daṇḍa tākṣyāsanaṃ śūlaṃ kharga mudgarameva ca
makaraṃ tripathaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ sthāṇurvā hastikarṇikam
bhīmaṃ vīrāsanaṃ cāpi vārāhaṃ mṛgavaiṇikam
ityetānyāsanānyatra saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyayā
dvitīyaḥ sajayaḥ prokto dhruvaṃ vyāhṛtimātṛbhiḥ
recakaḥ śūnyakaścaiva pūrakaḥ kumbhakastathā
evaṃ caturvidho bhedaḥ prāṇāyāme'tra sūribhiḥ
asūnāṃ nāḍayaḥ proktā gamāgamalayāśrayāḥ
recanācakaḥ proktaḥ śūnyakastu yathāsthitaḥ
pūraka pūraṇādvāyostanirodhācca kumbhakaḥ
dehino dakṣiṇe bhāge piṅgalā nāḍikā ramṛtā
dakṣiṇetaragā yā ca iḍā sā nāḍikā smṛtā
padmamūtranibhā nāḍī kāryākhyā brahmadaivatam
tataḥ śūnyaṃ nirālambaṃ madhye svātmani yojayet
vāhyasthādbodhanādvāyoḥ śūnyakatvaṃ vinirdiśet
āpyāyanaṃ bhavettena plāvanaṃ kalmaṣasya tu
aṅguṣṭhāgrātsamārabhya brahmarandhreṇa mocayet
saṃkocya kucikācakramūrdhvaṃ nītvā rasātrayam
saṃkṣobhya śaṅkhinīṃ samyaktato brahmaguhāṃ nayet
anena śodhayenmārgamaiśvaraṃ vimalaṃ muniḥ
sumukṣūṇāṃ sadā vatsa yogāṅgaṃ yogasiddhaye
vihāya vahnimārga tu aṅgulyāstu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
saumyenā''karṣayedvāyuṃ nābhāvākṛṣya dhārayet
jāyate vatsarādyogī jarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ
vāyumākarṣayedvāhyaṃ vāmayā codaraṃ bharet
nābhināsāntarā dhyāyaṃstriḥ prāṇāṃśca jayeddhruvam
manaḥ sthairya bhavedvatsa triṣu sthāneṣu dhāraṇāt
aṅguṣṭhanābhināsāgre vāyuṃ yogī jitāsanaḥ
apānaṃ kaṭideśe tu pṛṣṭhato vai vinirdiśet
nirālambe manaḥ kṛtvā kṣaṇātprāṇajito bhavet
indriyāṇāṃ vicaratāṃ viṣayeṣu svabhāvataḥ
karmendriyāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ pañcamādyetarejane
udvātāndaśa pañcaiva kārayeddhāraṇāṃ budhaḥ
prāṇavāyuṃ nivāyaiva manaḥ sūrye'ntare kṣipet
devāṃśca siddhāngandharvāśvāraṇānkhecarāngaṇān
ṣaṇmāsābhyāsayogena sūkṣmajyotiḥ prapaśyati
dṛṣṭe na syājjarā mṛtyuḥ sarvajñaśca prajāyate
sphoṭākhyā nāḍikā proktā kūrmalokastadāntare
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca vartamānaṃ ca dūrataḥ
jñānaṃ yattadbhavennūnaṃ sphoṭākhye jñānamabhyaset
lalāṭe mūrdhni hṛdaye sadāśivamanusmaret
dhyātvaivamātmani vibhuṃ dhyānaṃ tatsūrayo viduḥ
na jighrati na spṛśati na kiṃcidvā samīkṣate
guhyodarādisthāneṣu vāyuṃ nāsāṃ vicintayet
īśo'hamiti yogīndraḥ parānandaikavigrahaḥ
gamanāgamanābhyāṃ yo hīno vai viṣayojjhitaḥ
ekāntaronmanībhāvaḥ samādhirabhidhīyate
na sthūlaṃ na kṛśaṃ vā'pi na hrasvaṃ nāpi lopitam
na śuklaṃ nāpi vā pītaṃ na kṛṣṇaṃ nāpi karburram
kṛtvā hṛtpadmanilaye viśvākhyaṃ viśvasaṃbhavam
ātmānaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ parastāttamasaṃsthitam
pradhānapuruṣātītamākāśaṃ daharaṃ śivam
tadantaḥ sarvabhūtānāmīśvaraṃ brahmarūpiṇam
dhyāyedanādimadhyāntamānandādiguṇālayam
mahāntaṃ puruṣaṃ brahma brahmāṇaṃ brahma cāvyayam
oṃkārānte tathāsstmānaṃ saṃsthāpya paramātmani
ākāśe devamīśānaṃ dhyāyītā''kāśamadhyagam
kāraṇaṃ sarvabhāvānāmānandaikarasāśrayam
purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ śaṃbhuṃ dhyāyenmucyeta bandhanāt
mūḍho yathā śvalāṅgalaiḥ samudraṃ tartumicchati
tathā vinā śaṃbhusevāṃ saṃsārataraṇaṃ na hi
ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sūkṣmaṃ yatpaśyanti mumukṣavaḥ
pātuṃ tiṣṭhenmaheśena so'śnute yogamaiśvaram
naikalakṣaṃ dvilakṣaṃ vā trilakṣaṃ na mavātmakam
saṃsthāpya mayi cā''tmānaṃ paraṃ jyotiṣi nirguṇe
muhūrta tiṣṭhataḥ sākṣātasya cānubhavo bhavet
sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaśca jarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ
matprasādādbhavedyogī nānyathā krauñcasūdana
māmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ gacchedajñānaṃ nāśayāmyaham
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścānye ca saṃkarāḥ
madbhaktibhāvanāpūtā yānti matparamaṃ padam
yogināṃ karmiṇāṃ caiva tāpasānāṃ yatātmanām
ahameva gatisteṣāṃ nānyadastīti niśvayaḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure śivarakandasaṃvāde yamaniyama prāṇāyāmādikathanaṃ nāma dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
bhūtakāryayidaṃ dehamāpadrogākulaṃ param
viṣayaḥ pīḍyate deva sukha duḥkhātmakaiḥ sadā
abhibhūto yadā yogī duḥkhairadhyātmasaṃbhavaiḥ
yātanāyopasargāṇāṃ prasādādyogināṃ vada
īśvara uvāca
sāttvikā rājasā vighnāstāmasāstviha yoginām
prātibhāśravaṇāvārtādarśanāsvādavedanāḥ
daridro'hamahaṃ cā''ḍhyaḥ śūro'haṃ durbalastathā
mūrkho'haṃ ca suvidvāṃśca surūpo'hamarūpavān
dātā'haṃ kṛpaṇaścāhaṃ sukhī bhogyahameva ca
akulīnaḥ kulīnaśca kaṇṭakaḥ kaṇṭakojjhitaḥ
ahaṃkāramayaṃ kiṃcidyattatkṛtsnaṃ hi rājasam
andhatvaṃ caiva bādhirya paṅgatvaṃ duṣṭarogatā
śirorogo jvaraḥ śūlaiyakṣmamūrchā bhramādayaḥ
rājasāstāmasāḥ sarve tamohaṃkārasaṃyutāḥ
vyādhayo miśrabhāvena pīḍayantīha dehinam
kevalaṃ jāḍyabhāvena mūḍhatvaṃ mohana tathā
ajñānatvaṃ ca mūkatvamityādyāstāmasāḥ smṛtāḥ
gulakā yātudhānāca kiṃnaroragarākṣasāḥ
devadānava raudrāśca daityā mātarajā gaṇāḥ
tāmasāstu grahā bhūtā vāyubhūtā naraṃ sadā
pīḍayantīha vighnā hi yogābhyāsarataṃ grahaiḥ
evamādyupasargāṇāṃ vāraṇāya ca dhāraṇām
vakṣyāmi vividhāṃ vatsa yogināṃ siddhihetave
tvagādisaptadhātūnāmekībhūtaṃ vicintayet
praṇavaṃ kaṇṭhanāsāgre sabījaṃ vahnidīpitam
pittarogābhibhūto vā yogī yogaparāyaṇaḥ
praviśya brahmarūpeṇa deha nirvāṇajaṃ smaret
paittikāśropasargāya mānunā timiraṃ yathā
nāśayedandhatāṃ yogī divyadṛṣṭiḥ prajāyate
pītvā pārthivataśvena svambhaṃ vāyorvināśayet
puṣṭirevātulā tasya sthirasvaṃ rujahīnatā
śrotramākāśavāyvośca atraikatvaṃ vicintayet
śṛṇoti dūrataḥ sarva śrutaghārī bhavetsadā
viyanmayo'tha saṃcārī satatābhyāsayogataḥ
saroja rasanāyāṃ ca taddraṣṭāraṃ sakarṇikam
prajñā caivaṃ smṛtirmedhā kavitvaṃ buddhiruttamā
stambhanaṃ duṣṭatvānāṃ sarvavāyuñjayetsadā
hṛtsarojagataṃ devamaṣṭādaśabhujairyutam
nīlāruṇaṃ mahākārya kcindrajaṭādharam
siṃhacarmāmbaraṃ bhīmaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
bhujaṅgamhārābharaṇaṃ sarvakaṅkanūpuram
jvālāmālākulaṃ dīsaṃ bhābhāsitadigānanam
tayathāvṛṣṭama tre tu tasminnai maneneotyāpayetkṣaṇāt
lakṣamādhāya tatraiva yojayenmāye ṣaṇmukha
ghṛtaṃ ghṛteṣveva yatha niyuktaṃ prayāti caikyādaviśeṣabhāvam
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure śivaskandasaṃvāde sāttvikarājasa vighnādikathanaṃ nāma trayodaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
bavāni saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
tatra kṛṣṇāṣṭamī puṇyā sarvapāpapraṇāśanī
kamasaśita pustakeṣu ya ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ sa evātra saṃgṛhītaḥ
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvratānnānyadvatamasti vibhūtidam
kṛṣṇāṣṭamītrataṃ kṛtvā brahmā brahmatvamāpnuyāt
viṣṇutvaṃ prāptavānviṣṇuḥ sureśatvaṃ śacīpatiḥ
candraścandratvamāpanno gaṇeśatvaṃ gaṇādhipaḥ
rakandaḥ senāpatitvaṃ ca tathā cānye gaṇeśvarāḥ
kṛtvā caiśvaryamāpannāḥ saubhāgyaṃ devavallabhāḥ
vratasyāsya prabhāvena lakṣmyāḥ patirabhūddhariḥ
yayātiḥ sārvabhaumatvaṃ tathā cānye nṛpottamāḥ
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhā gandharvāṇāṃ ca kanyakāḥ
kṛtvā caiva parāṃ siddhiṃ prāptāśca munipuṅgavāḥ
nandīśvareṇa yatproktaṃ nāradāya mahātmane kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam
meroryadākṣiṇaṃ śṛṅgaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam
tatra nandīśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvajñaṃ śaṃbhuvallabham
upāsyamānaṃ munibhiḥ stūyamānaṃ marudgaṇaiḥ
abravītpraṇipatyātha daṇḍavannārado muniḥ
nārada uvāca
saubhāgyaṃ kāntimaiśvaryamapatyaṃ ca yaśastathā
śāśvatīṃ muktimante ca paśupāśavimocanīm
bhagavaṃstadvrataṃ brūhi kāruṇyācchaṃkarabhiyam
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ śreṣṭhamasti devaṛṣe śṛṇu gaṇeśatvaṃ mayā labdhaṃ yena cīrṇena nārada
māse mārgaśire prāpte kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ jitendriyaḥ
aśvatthadantakāṣṭhena kṛtvā vai dantadhāvanam
snānaṃ kṛtvā ca vidhivattarpaṇaṃ caiva nārada
āgatya bhavanaṃ paścātpūjayecchaṃkaraṃ prabhum
gomūtraṃ prāśya vidhivadupavāsī bhavenniśi
atirātrasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet
pūjayecchaṃ bhunāmānaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram
vājapeyāṣṭakaphalaṃ prāpnoti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
māghe vaṭasya kathitaṃ gokṣīraṃ prāśanaṃ smṛtam
māheśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya gomedhasyāṣṭakaṃ phalam
phālgune ca tadevoktaṃ kāryaṃ vai prāśanaṃ ca tat
saṃpūjayenmahādevaṃ rājasūyāṣṭakaṃ phalam
kāṣṭhamaudumbaraṃ caitre prāśane varjitā janāḥ it pūjayetsthāṇunāmānamaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
śivaṃ saṃpūjya vaiśākhe pītvā caiva kuśodakam
naramedhāṣṭaphalaṃ prāpnotyeva hi nārada
jyeṣṭhe lākṣaṃ bhavetkāṣṭhaṃ pūjyaḥ paśupatirvibhuḥ
gavāṃ śṛṅgodakaṃ prāśya svapedevasya saṃnidhau
gavāṃ koṭipradānasya yatpuṇyaṃ tadavāpnuyāt
āṣāḍhe cogranāmānamiṣṭvā prāśya ca gomayam
sautrāmaṇyāstu yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet
pālāśaṃ śrāvaṇe proktaṃ śarteṃ saṃpūjya nārada
prāśayitvā'rkapatrāṇi kalpaṃ śivapure vaset
māse bhādrapade'ṣṭamyāṃ tryambakaṃ saṃprapūjayet
māśanaṃ bilvapatrasya sarvadīkṣāphalaṃ bhavet
āśvine jambuvṛkṣasya dantakāṣṭhamudīritam
īśvaraṃ pūjayedbhaktyā prāśayettaṇḍulodakam
pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ labhet
māse tu kārtike'ṣṭamyāmīśānākhyaṃ prapūjayet
pañcagavyaṃ sakṛtpītvā agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet
varṣānte bhojayedviprā śivabhaktiparāyaṇān
śaktyā hiraṇyaṃ vāsāṃsi bhaktyā tebhyo nivedayet
saratnāṃ tāmrakalaśīṃ gāmalaṃkṛtya nārada
alaṃkāraṃ ca vastraṃ ca dakṣiṇāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ samyakprāptaṃ devaṛṣe mayā
sūta uvāca
evaṃ nandīśvarācchrutvā nārado munipuṅgavāḥ
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ puṇyaṃ yayau badarikāśramam
vratasyāsya prabhāvaṃ yaḥ paṭhedvā śṛṇuyādapi
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde kṛṣṇāṣṭamī vrataṃ nāma caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
yaduktaṃ bhānunā pūrva yājñavalkyāya yogine
yājñavalkya uvāca
jayā ca vijayā caiva kiṃphalā kiparāyaṇā
tasyāṃ viśiṣṭaṃ yatpuṇyaṃ vada kaśyapanandana
sūrya uvāca
dvādaśī viṣṇudayitā dvādaśī vaiṣṇavī tithiḥ
śuklapakṣe dvijaśreṣṭha vijayā sā prakīrtitā
upoṣyā sā prayatnena sarvapāpapraṇāśanī
yā tu puṣyeṇa saṃyuktā phālgunasya sitā tu vai
sā jayā dvādaśī nāma sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī
tasyāṃ snātaḥ sadā snāto bhavedvai nātra saṃśayaḥ
saṃpūjya vastrapuṣpādyaiḥ phalaṃ sāyaṃ samaśnute
ṛcamekāmadhīte yo vimaḥ śraddhāsamanvitaḥ
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu
yaśvopavāsaṃ kurute tasyāṃ snāto dvijottama
yaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśīmimāṃ kṣapayedbhaktimānnaraḥ
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇumarcayet
matsyā pādau prathamaṃ kūrmāya ca tathā kaṭim
varāhāyeti jaṭharaṃ narasiṃhāya vā uraḥ
vāmanāyeti vai kaṇṭhaṃ bhujaṃ rāmadvayeti ca
kṛṣṇanāmnā ca netre dve buddhanāmnā tathā śiraḥ
bhaktyā cāssrādhya govindaṃ gopālaṃ ca tathā niśi
tatastasyāgrataḥ śuddhaṃ nyasetkṛṣṇājinaṃ budhaḥ
tasyopari tilānāṃ tu kṛṣṇānāmāḍhakaṃ nyaset
tilālābhe yavāḥ kāryā godhūmāratadalābhataḥ
sauvarṇa raupyaṃ tāmraṃ vā pātraṃ kuryātsvaśaktitaḥ
pracchādya pātraṃ vāsobhirahataiḥ suparīkṣitaiḥ
sauvarṇa vāmanaṃ kṛtvā sākṣasūtra kamaṇḍalum
yathāśaktyā kṛtaṃ haravaṃ kṛtayajñopavītinam
evaṃrūpaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā vāmanaṃ bhaktimānnaraḥ
matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca nārasiṃho'tha vāmanaḥ
rāmo rāmaśca kṛṣṇaśca buddhaḥ kalkī ca te daśa
bhaktasyātra viśeṣeṇa phalaṃ koṭiguṇottaram
chatraṃ caivākṣasūtraṃ ca pāduke guḍikāṃ tathā
jāgaraṃ tatra kurvīta gītavādināditaiḥ
pradeyaṃ śāstraviduṣe brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine
viṣṇubhaktāya śāntāya viśeṣeṇa dīyate
vedādhyetre samaṃ dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ tadvide tathā
ācārye dānamekaṃ ca sahastraguṇitaṃ tathā
evaṃ dattvā vidhānena brāhmaṇāya ca bhaktitaḥ
mantreṇānena dātavyaṃ purāṇapaṭhitena ca
mantreṇa pratigṛhṇīyādbrāhmaṇaśca dvijottama
vāmano'sya pradātā vai vāmanāya namo namaḥ iti dānamantraḥ
vāmanaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vāmano vai dadāti ca
vāmanastārako dvābhyāṃ vāmanāya namo namaḥ
annaṃ prajāpatirviṣṇurudrendraśaśibhāskarāḥ
parjanyo varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ salilaṃ keśavaḥ śivaḥ
svaṣṭā yamo vaiśravaṇaḥ pāpaṃ haratu me sadā
viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ dattvā yathāśaktyatha dakṣiṇām
pṛṣadājyaṃ ca saṃprāśya paścādbhuñjīta vāgyataḥ
bhūyo yathecchayā rātrau sarvatraiṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
brahmalokādilokeṣu bhuktvā bhogānanekaśaḥ
punaḥ svargādbhuvaṃ prāpya jāyate mahatāṃ kule
saptadvīpādhipatyaṃ ca prāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ
itīdaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ paṭhevatamanuttamam
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ śravaṇadvādaśīphalāt
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtayājñavalkyasaṃvāde śravaṇa dvādaśīvratakathanaṃ nāma pañcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
anyadvratamidaṃ vakṣye śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
saubhāgyavardhanaṃ puṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam
sarvaduṣṭopaśamanaṃ sarvaiśvaryamadaṃ śivam
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
purā devena rudreṇa dagdhaḥ kāmo durāsadaḥ
upoṣitā tithistena tenānaṅgatrayodaśī
śuklapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ māsi mārgaśire dvijāḥ
snānaṃ kṛtvā'tha vidhinā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ
śaṃbhunānā tilaihoṃmaṃ kuryādaṣṭottaraṃ śatam
anaṅganāmnā saṃpūjya madhu prāśya svapenniśi
daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
yogeśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya pauṣe prāśrīta candanam
rājasūyasya yajñasya phailamānoti mānavaḥ
nāṭeśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya māghamāse jitendriyaḥ
mauktikaṃ prāśya viprendrāḥ phalaṃ tasya vadāmyaham
saṃpūjya phālgune vīraṃ kaḍūnelaṃ prāśayonārī
vaiśākhe ca mahārūpaṃ deveśaṃ ca prapūjayet
jātīphalaṃ ca saṃprāśya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet
jyeṣṭhe pradyumnanāmānaṃ lavaṅgaṃ prāśayenniśi
umābhartetināmānamāṣāḍhe saṃprapūjayet
tilodakaṃ tu saṃprāśya puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet
pūjayecchrāvaṇe śūlapāṇinaṃ parameśvaram
māse bhādrapade vimāḥ sadyojātaṃ prapūjayet
agaruṃ prāśayitvā tu sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
māse cāśvayuje prāpte tridaśādhipatiṃ yajet
svarṇodakaṃ tu saṃprāśya svarṇakoṭiphalaṃ labhet
viśveśvaraṃ ca kārtikyāṃ pūjayedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ
pratimāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi dantakāṣṭhāni vai dvijāḥ
mallikā khādiraṃ caiva lakṣāpāmārgajaṃ tathā
jambudumbarajāśvatthaṃ mālatī vaṭajaṃ tathā
mālatyāḥ prathamaṃ tāvattato marutrakaṃ tathā
karavīraṃ tathā kundamarkapatrāṇi suvratāḥ
tato mandārapuṣpāṇi mallikākusumāni ca
kādambaṃ yūthikāpuṣpaṃ dhatturaṃ śatapatrakam
durvāṅkurāṇi deyāni naivedyāni yathākramam
odanaṃ kṛśaraṃ caina śarkarāmodakāstathā
kaṃsāraṃ yāvakāstatra tataḥ sauhālikā bhavet
pañcakhādyaṃ paraṃ proktaṃ ghṛtapūramanantaram
nānāvidhānaṃ naivedyaṃ kārtikyāṃ parikalpayet
pūjānāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
śaṃkarāya namaḥ pādau gauye gulphe śivāya ca
śivāyai jānunī pūjya śaṃbhavāyodbhavāya ca
kaiṭiṃ manmathanāśāya madanāyai surerśvare
nābhi bhavāya saṃpūjya bhavānyai nama ityumām
vakṣo devādhidevāya aparṇāyai namaḥ śivām
kaṇṭha bhīmograrūpāya girijāyai namaḥ śivām
skandhaṃ tridaśavandyāya triśūlinyai namaḥ śivām
bāhū dhūrjayetyuktvā dhūsarāyai namaḥ śivām
hastau śūladharāyeti śūlinyai nama ityumām
mukhaṃ devasya saṃpūjya vāmadeveti vāstaḥ
vāmāyai nama ityuktvā nāsāṃ caiva kapāline
mṛḍānyai nama ityuktvā lalāṭaṃ cendudhāriṇe
alakāyai namaḥ paścātrinetrāya namastathā
tryakṣyai saṃpūjayedevīṃ śiro gaṅgādharāya ca
kātyāyanīṃ tataḥ pūjya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ
keśānsaṃpūjya vidhivatkeśinyai ca namo namaḥ
śuklavastreṇa saṃchādya saṃpūjya vidhivadvijāḥ
ācāryāyātha taṃ dadyādvittaśāyyavivarjitaḥ
kalaśāḥ sodakā deyā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sadakṣiṇāḥ
brāhmaṇānbhojayedbhaktyā śivabhaktiparāyaṇān
evaṃ karoti yo viprā bhaktyā'naṅgatrayodaśīm
prāpnoti rājyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ putrāṃśca cirajīvinaḥ
śivalokaṃ ca saṃprāpya śaṃbhoḥ priyatamo bhavet
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde'naṅgatrayodaśī vratakathanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
yaduktaṃ bhavatā sūta naiṣkalaṃ jñānamuttamam
śrutaṃ cākhilamasmābhirmanāṃsi hṛṣitāni naḥ
bhaktiśca śāśvate śaṃbhau jātā'smākaṃ hi śāśvatī
varṇāśramācāravidhimidānīṃ brūhi tattvataḥ
sūta uvāca
caturṇāmapi varṇānāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi suvratāḥ
yaduktaṃ bhānunā pūrve manave parameṣṭhine
yena viśveśvaraḥ śaṃbhuḥ karmayogarataiḥ sadā
ārādhyate na cānyena ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaśturthaḥ śūdra ucyate
varṇāścatvāra evaite traya ādyā dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ
catvāraśvā''śramārateṣāṃ pañcamo nopapadyate
sarveṣāmāśramāṇāṃ ca vihitaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam
na daṇḍena vinā kaśvidāśramīti nigadyate
brahmacārī bhaveddaṇḍī kṛṣṇājinadharaistathā
mekhalī ca tathā muṇḍī śikhī vā yadi vā jaṭī
bhikṣāhāreṇa satataṃ vartanaṃ tasya suvratāḥ
agnikārya tathā kuryātsāyaṃ prātaryathāvidhi
snātvā saṃtarpya devādīndevatābhyarcanaṃ tataḥ
abhivādanaśīlaḥ syādvṛddheṣu ca yathākramam
ādhyātmikaṃ vaidikaṃ vā tathā laukikameva vā
ādadīta guroryasmāttaṃ pūrvamabhivādayet
asāvahamiti brūyātpratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ
nābhivāyāstu vipreṇa kṣatriyādyāḥ kathaṃcana
śiṣṭānāṃ ca gṛhānnityaṃ bhikṣāmāhṛtya suvrataḥ
nivedya gurave'śrīyādvāgyatastadanujñayā
bhaikṣeṇa vartanaṃ nityaṃ naikānnādī vratī bhavet
upavāsasamā bhikṣā proktā vai brahmacāriṇām
prāṅmukho'nnādi bhuñjīta sūryābhimukha eva vā
nābādadaṅmukho nityaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ
bhuñjīta maunī satataṃ smaredevaṃ sadāśivam
sopānatko jalastho vā noṣṇīṣī cā''camedbudhaḥ
prāśnīyātrirapaḥ pūrvaṃ brāhmaṇa prayato dvijaḥ
saṃvṛttā mūlena mukhaṃ caivamupaspṛśet
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśennayanadvayam
aṅguṣṭhatarjanībhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśenāsikāpuṭe
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayogena spṛśecchratrayugaṃ dvijaḥ
sarvābhiraṅgulībhiśca hṛdayaṃ ca talena vā
saṃspṛśedvai śirastadvadaṅguṣṭhenāthavā dvayam
divā mūtrapurīṣe ca śarvaryā dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ
ācchādya parṇairvasudhāṃ tṛṇairvā maunasaṃyutaḥ
śiraḥ prāhṛtya viprendrā nānyathā ca kadācana
pathi goṣṭhe nadītīre chāyāyāṃ kūpasaṃnidhau
tuṣāṅgārakapāleṣu na kṣetre na catuṣpathe
nodyāne na śmaśāne ca na paśyaṃstārakādikān
na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayorgavām
śaucaṃ paścātprakurvīta gandhalepakṣayāvadhi
āntaraṃ manasaḥ śuddhiryathā bhavati tadvijāḥ
jitendriyaḥ syātsatataṃ vaśyātmā'krodhanaḥ śuciḥ
prayuñjīta sadā vācaṃ madhurāṃ hitabhāṣiṇīm
dyūtaṃ janaparīvādaṃ strī velyālambhanaṃ tathā
sarva paryuṣitaṃ varṇya kṛtaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ tathā
malāpakarṣaṇaṃ snānaṃ śūdrādyairabhibhāṣaṇam
guroravajñāṃ satataṃ brahmacārī vivarjayet
udakumbhaṃ sumanaso gośakṛnmṛttikī kuśān
ācamya saṃyato nityamadhīyīta chudaṅmukhaḥ
upasaṃgṛhya tatpādau vīkṣamāṇo gurormukham
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vedaścakṣuḥ sanātanam
vedaḥ śreyaskaraḥ puṃsāṃ nānya ityabravīdraviḥ
anadhītya dvijo yastu śāstrāṇi subahūnyapi
śṛṇoti brāhmaṇo nāsau narakāṇi prapadyate
nāsscāraphalamāpnoti yathā śūdrastathaiva saḥ
śūdraputraḥ sa vijñeyāṃ na vedaphalamaśrute
vedaṃ vedau tathā vedavedāṃśca caturo dvijāḥ
adhītya guruve dattvā dakṣiṇāṃ ca bhavedgṛhī
rūpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktāṃ kanyāmuddāhayettataḥ
amātṛgotraprabhavāmasamānārṣagotrajām
mātṛtaḥ pañcamādūrdhvaṃ pitṛtaḥ saptamāttathā
agotrakula saṃpanna rogahīnāṃ surūpiṇīm
mātṛtaḥ pañcamādavapitṛttaḥ saptamāttathā
dhārayedvaiṇavīṃ yaṣṭimantarvāsastathottaram
yajñopavītadvitayaṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum
chatraṃ coṣṇīpamamalaṃ pāduke vā'pyupāna hau
raukme ca kuṇḍale nityaṃ kṛttakeśanakhaḥ śuciḥ
paṣṭaṣṭamyau pañcadaśīmamāvāsyāṃ caturdaśīm
brahmacārī bhavennityaṃ janma ca viśeṣataḥ
ādadītā''vasathyāgniṃ juhuyājjātavedasam
akurvāṇaḥ patatyāśu nirayānatibhīṣaṇān
kuryādrahmāṇi karmāṇi saṃdhyopāsanameva ca
vaiṣavānbuddhisādṛśyamācaranvicaretsadā
tamācāraṃ niṣeveta sādhūnvakṣyāmi sāṃpratam
yastairanuṣṭhito dharmaḥ śrutismṛtyo saṃgataḥ
sadācāraḥ sa vai prokto devadevena śaṃbhunā
kurukṣetrāśca matsyārthe pāñcālāḥ śūrasenajāḥ
ete deśāḥ puṇyadeśāḥ sarve cānye ca ninditāḥ
deśepaveṣu nivasedrāhmaṇairdharmakāṅkṣibhiḥ
aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgāṃśca saurāṣṭraṃ gurjaraṃ tathā
ābhīraṃ kauḍūṇaṃ caiva drāviḍaṃ dakṣiṇāpatham
andhaṃ ca māgadhaṃ caiva deśānetāṃśca varjayet
nityaṃ svādhyāyaśīlaḥ syātpañcayajñaparāyaṇaḥ
sāvitrījāpyanirataḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ
śrāddhakṛddānanirataḥ kṣamāyukto dayālukaḥ
gṛhasthastu samākhyāto na gṛheṇa gṛhī bhavet
na śarīraṃ vinā devaḥ pūjyate girijāpatiḥ
brahmacārī gṛhastho vā vānaprastho'thavā yatiḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde varṇāśramācāra vidhikathanaṃ māma saptadaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
vadenaivābhiyaṃ vākyaṃ nānṛtaṃ na ca marmabhit
na hiṃsyātsarvabhūtāni na vedānāṃ ca kutsanam
nindakānāṃ maheśasya śuddhirna khalu dṛśyate
jalaṃ tṛṇaṃ vā śākaṃ vā mṛdaṃ vā kāṣṭhameva vā
prāṇānapaharatyeṣa yācakastasya durmatiḥ
grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi devārcanavidhau dvijaiḥ
tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai haredbudhaḥ
tilamudrayavādīnāṃ muṣṭiryādyā yadi sthitaiḥ
anṛtātpāradāryācca tathā'bhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇāt
pūrvaḥ pūrvo'bhivādyaḥ syātpūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ
tripuṇḍradhārī satataṃ brāhmaṇaḥ sarvakarmasu
na mūkhaiḥ saha saṃvāsaḥ patitairna kadācana
paiśunyaṃ śuṣkavairāṇi vivādaṃ varjayetsadā
dhayantīṃ gāṃ parakṣetre na cā''cakṣīta kasyacit
tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyānakṣatrāṇi na nirdiśet
na pāpaṃ pāpināṃ brūyāttathā'pāpamapāpinām
yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patantyaśrṛṇi rodanāt
tāni putrānpaśūnghnanti teṣāṃ mithyābhiśaṃsinām
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaṅgannāgamaḥ
dṛṣṭaṃ virodhanaṃ vṛddhairnārita midhyābhiśaṃsini
mānaṃ madaṃ tathā śokaṃ dveṣaṃ ca parivarjayet
ravivāre na kurvīta bhṛṣṭabhairavabhakṣaṇam
dhanakāmo janaḥ satyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
na kuryātkasyacitpīḍāṃ sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet
na nadīṣu nadīṃ brūyātparvateṣu ca parvatam
śirobhyaṅgāvaśiṣṭena tailenāṅgaṃ na lepayet
ne sarpaśastraiḥ krīḍeta svāni khāni na saṃspṛśet
na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kaṇḍūyedātmanaḥ śiraḥ
nāśuddho' paricarena devānkīrtaye dṛṣīn
viśveśvaramumākāntaṃ viśvāntaryāmiṇaṃ vibhum
na brahmādyaiḥ samaṃ brūyācchaktibhirna ca pārvatīm
brūyādyadi samaṃ śaṃbhuṃ brahmaviṣṇvādibhiḥ suraiḥ
yaḥ kaścittamasā''viṣṭaḥ kadācinnaiva taṃ spṛśet
tathā devīṃ ca girijāṃ dvijaiḥ śreyorthibhiḥ sadā
parastriyaṃ na bhāṣeta nāyājyaṃ yājayedvijāḥ
na cāsskāmedgurośchāyāṃ na tatho''jñāṃ guroḥ sadā
vakṣyamāṇena vidhinā snānaṃ kuryātsamāhitaḥ
bhūmiṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ spṛṣṭrā khanamānaṃ dhru cāśayā
uddhṛtā'sīti saṃgṛhya gandhadvāreti gomayam
apāghamityapāmārga dūrvā saṃgṛhya durvayā
jalatīraṃ samāsādya śucau deśe samāhitaḥ
ādityā iti saṃprokṣya kūlaṃ tīrthasya suvrataḥ
śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya gāyatryā prokṣayettataḥ
bhāgadvayaṃ sa tāṃ paścādekaṃ dikṣu visarjayet
avaśiṣṭena bhāgena mantraiśvā''lepayetkramāt
akṣībhyāmitimantreṇa mukhamālepayedbudhaḥ
grīvābhyāmiti ca grīvāṃ tallina tathā bhujau
śarīraṃ yajñamuktvā'tha hṛdayaṃ parilepayet
nābhimānandanandeti śiṣṭaṃ mūrdhni vinikṣipet
mūrdhānamitimantreṇa tiladūrvākṣatādikam
hiraṇyaśṛṅgamityuktvā tīrthaṃ saṃprārthya buddhimān japecchuddhamatiḥ paścātsūktaṃ caivāghamarṣaṇam
dvipadāṃ ca japedevīṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanīm
idaṃ tu vāruṇaṃ snānaṃ mantrasnānamathocyate
tu āgneyaṃ bhasmanā snānaṃ vāyavyaṃ rajasā mavām
ārdreṇa vāsasā cānyanmānasaṃ śivacintanam
svānānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ mānasaṃ snānamuttamam
traivarṇikānāṃ sarveṣāṃ gāyatrī paramā gatiḥ
yadgāyatryāḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ
iti jñātvā japedvidvān gāyatryāḥ phalamaśnute
yo hyanyathā tu manute gāyatrī śivarūpiṇīm
pādācatvāro gāyatryā vedācatvāra eva te
viraściviṣṇusdeśāḥ pādānāṃ devatāḥ kramāt
evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena gāyatrī vedamātaram japenmāheśvaraṃ jyotirnityameva prakāśate
upatiṣṭhedathā''dityaṃ rudrarūpiṇamavyayam
pāvamānāni sūktāni brahmayajñaprasiddhaye
japetsamāhito bhūtvā rudrāṃścaiva viśeṣataḥ
ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa mānastokyā tathaiva ca
nāstītyuvāca bhagavāndevadevaḥ svayaṃ raviḥ
nāsaṃpūjya mahādevaṃ bhuñjīta brāhmaṇaḥ sadā
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ karmiṇāṃ yogināmapi
kuryātpañca mahāyajñāngṛhasthaḥ śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
pañcayajñaparityāgādāśramoṃdavahīyate
devayajño bhūtayajñaḥ pitṛyajñastathā'paraḥ
mānuṣo brahmayajñaśca pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
hutaśeṣeṇa bhūtebhyo bālaṃ bhūtamakhaṃ viduḥ
nityaśrāddhaṃ tadṛddhiṃ pitṛyajñaṃ pracakṣate
yathāśaktyannumudṛtya padadyādrāhmaṇāya vai
atithiṃ pūjayedbhaktyā śivabhāvasamanvitaḥ
madadyādvratakāraṃ vā bhikṣāṃ ca bhavabhāvataḥ
etānkṛtvaiva satataṃ bhuñjītā''śramedharmabhiḥ
anyathā yo hi bhuṅkte'nnaṃ pretya śūkaratāṃ vrajet
yadi viśveśvare sthāṇī bhaktirekaiva niścalā
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde dvijadharma kathanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
śrāddhaṃ darśe'tha kartavyamaṣṭakāsvayanadvaye
viṣuve ca vyatīpāte tīrtheṣu ca viśeṣataḥ
parīkṣya brāhmaṇānsamyagvedavedāṅgapāragān
viśeṣācchivabhaktāṃśca rudrajāpyaparāyaṇān
abhāve śivabhaktānāṃ sadācāraratāndvijān
bhojayecchraddhayā śrāddhe śivabuddhayā samāhitaḥ
vratopavāsaniratāḥ somapāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ
agnihotraparāḥ śāntā vahcā gurupūjakāḥ
triṇāciketāḥ śiṣyāśca trimadhutrisuparṇikāḥ
mantrabrāhmaṇavettāraḥ purāṇaramṛtipāṭhakāḥ
adhyātmaśāstraniratā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ
ekaṃ vā bhojayedvimaṃ śivabhaktiparāyaṇam
tena pūtā bhavantyeva ye kecitpaṅktidūṣakāḥ
vadhabandhopajīvī ca vṛṣalaḥ śūdrayojakāḥ
vedavikrayiṇaścānye kopinaḥ kuṇḍagolakau
kāyasthā lambakarṇāśca nityaṃ rājopasevakāḥ
nakṣatratithivaktāro bhiṣakśāstropajīvinaḥ
vyādhinaḥ kāvyakartāro gāyakācaiva gotriṇaḥ
vedanindāratāścaiva kṛtaghnāḥ piśunāstathā
hīnātirikta dehāśca śrāddhe varjyāḥ prayatnataḥ
adhvānaṃ kalahaṃ krodhaṃ putrabhāryāditāḍanam
prakṣālayettataḥ pādāvarcite maṇḍale śubhe
vartulaṃ caitra vaiśyasya śūdrasyābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
paścācchrāddhasya rakṣārthaṃ tilāṃśca vikirettataḥ
viśvedevānathā''hūya viśvedevāsa ityṛcā
śaṃnodevyā jalaṃ kṣiptvā sapavitre tu bhājane
yavānyavo'sīti tathā gandhapuṣpaṃ ca nikṣipet
madadyādgandhamālyādi dhūpaṃ vāsāṃsi śaktitaḥ
apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṛnāvāhayettataḥ
uśantastvati ca ṛcā āvāhya tadanujñayā
japedāyantu na ṛcaṃ tilo'sīti nilāṃstathā
pitṛbhyaḥ sthānamasīti tato'naukaraṇaṃ matam
mahādevasya purato goṣṭhe vā śraddhayā'nvitaḥ
piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāṃcaiva bhojayet
vividhaṃ pāyasaṃ dadyādbhakṣyāṇi subahūnyapi
lehyaṃ coṣyaṃ tathā kāmapuṣpameva phalaṃ vinā
vividhānyapi māṃsāni pitṛṇāṃ prītipūrvakam
dattānyapi niṣiddhāni śrāddhaṃ naivākṣayaṃ bhavet
nāśnāti yo dvijo māṃsaṃ niyuktaḥ pitṛkarmaṇi
dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ ca tathā'tharvaśirastathā
rudrāṃśca pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ brāhmaṇāñśrāvayettataḥ
bhuñjīranbrāhmaṇāḥ sarve vāgyatā ghṛtabhojanāḥ
vikiraṃ nikṣipetpaścāccheṣamannamathābravīt
dādvai dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā svadhākāramudīrayet
dātāro no'bhivardhantāṃ vājevājeti vai ṛcam
bhoktā ca śrāddhadaratasyāṃ rajanyāṃ maithunaṃ tyajet
adhvago vyasanī caiva viśeṣeṇa hānagnikaḥ
āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijaḥ kuryāddurbarlaṃstu sadaiva hi
śraddhayā tu kṛte śrāddhe bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure mṛtaśaunakasaṃvāde śrāddhavidhi kathanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
atha dharmo vanasthānāmucyate śṛṇuta dvijāḥ
śarīramātmano dṛṣṭvā palitāyaiśca dūṣitam
phalamūlāśano nityaṃ pañcayajñaparāyaṇaḥ
atithiṃ pūjayedbhaktyā matvā śarva iti śrutiḥ
aṣṭau grāsāṃśca bhuñjīta cīravāsā bhavejjaṭī
bhavetriṣavaṇastrāyī nityaṃ svādhyāyatatparaḥ
dayāṃ ca sarvabhūteṣu na kuryānniśi bhojanam
varjayedgrāmajātāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
yadi gacchedvanī bhāryā prāyaścittī bhavedvijaḥ
ādigarbho bhavettasyāḥ sa cāṇḍālasamo bhavet
sarvabhūtānukampī syātsaṃvibhānarataḥ sadā
parivādaṃ mṛpāvādaṃ nidrālasyaṃ vivarjayet
śīrṇaparṇāśano vā syātkṛcchrava vartayetsadā
śivapūjārato nityaṃ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
parāṃ gatimavāpnoti dehānte śāśvataṃ padam
vedāntābhyāsanirato dāntaḥ śānto jitendriyaḥ
jīrṇakaupīnavāsāḥ syānmuṇḍo nagno'thavā bhavet
tridaṇḍī vā bhavedvidvānityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ
samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā mānāpamānayoḥ
ekānnādī bhavedyastu kadācillampaṭo yatiḥ
niṣkṛtinaiva tasyāsti dharmaśāstreṣu sarvathā bhavetriṣavaṇasnāyī bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ
anantaṃ nirguṇaṃ śāntaṃ puruṣaṃ prakṛteḥ param
kāraṇa sarvajagatāmādhāraṃ sarvatomukham
cidrūpaṃ śaṃkareṃ sthāṇumānandamajaraṃ vibhum
jñānī mokṣamavāpnoti virāṭpadamakhe rataḥ
iti sarvamaśeṣeṇa cāturāśramyamīritam
ici śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunaka saṃvāde vānaprasthādidharmakathanaṃ nāma viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
manvantarāṇi vaiśātha teṣāṃ ca caritaṃ tathā
pratisargaḥ punaścaiva yathā bhavati kṛtstraṃśaḥ
brūhi naḥ sūca sakale yathā nyāsācchrutaṃ tvayā sūta uvāca
śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve svecchālīlāṃ maheśituḥ
kṣobhyaṃ viśvamidaṃ tena kṣobhako bhagavāśivaḥ
sa saṃkoca vikāśābhyāṃ pradhānatve vyavasthitaḥ
kṣobhyamānātpradhānācca puṃsaḥ prādurabhūdvijāḥ
yadetadvistṛtaṃ bījaṃ pradhānapuruṣātmakam
buddhyādaya viśeṣāntā avyaktādīśvarecchyā
puruṣādhiṣṭhitādeva jajñire munipuṃgavāḥ
ahaṃkārastato jajñe tanmātrāṇi tato dvijāḥ
tato bhūtāni jātāni preritāni śivecchayā
vaikārikādahaṃkārātsargo vaikāriko bhavet
taijasānīndriyāṇyāhurdevā vaikārikā daśa
vaikārikāttaijesaśca bhūtādicaiva tāmasaḥ
bhūtāderabhavatsargo bhūtatanmātrasaṃjñitaḥ
vikurvāṇastu bhūtoṃdiḥ śabdamātraṃ sasarja ha ākāśo jāyate tasmāttasya śabdo guṇo mataḥ
pavanaśca vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha
tejaśvotpadyate tasmādrūpaṃ tasya guṇaṃ viduḥ
tejastveva vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātramabhūttataḥ
utpadyante tataścā''po rasastāsāṃ guṇo mataḥ
gandhācca pṛthivī jātā gandhastasyāstu vai guṇaḥ śabdamātraṃ yadākāśaṃ sparśamātraṃ samādṛṇot
dviguṇaḥ procyate vāyuḥ śabdasparśātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ
tathaiva viyato rūpaṃ śabdasparśo guṇāvubhau
tejastataḥ syātriguṇaṃ saśabdasparśarūpavat
rasamātraṃ guṇāḥ sarve traya ādyāḥ samāviśan
āpaścaturguṇāstena gandhamātraṃ samāviśan
tasmātpañcaguṇā bhūmirbalā bhūteṣu kathyate
puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca
mahadādiviśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te
tasminkāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prākṛte'ṇḍe virañcistu kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ
ādikartā sa bhūtānāṃ brahmā'gre samavartata
merurulbaṃ bhavettasya jarāyuścāpi parvatāḥ
garbhodakaṃ samudrāśca tasyā''sanparameṣṭhinaḥ
viśva tatrābhavadviprāḥ sadevāsuramānuṣam
adbhirdaśaguṇābhistu bāhyato'ṇḍaṃ samāhṛtam
āpo daśaguṇenaiva tejasā bahirāvṛtāḥ
tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunā''vṛtam
ākāśenāssvṛto vāyuḥ khaṃ tu bhūtādinā''vṛtam
mahatā caiva bhūtādiravyaktenāssvṛto mahān
etairāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prākṛtairvṛtam
guṇāḥ kālavaśādeva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ
guṇasāmye layo jñeyo vaiṣamye sṛṣṭirucyate
brahmāṇḍameva viprendrā brahmaṇaḥ kṣetramucyate
kṣetrajñaśca sa evokto virañciśva prajāpatiḥ
sahasrakoṭayaḥ santi brahmāṇḍāstiryagūrdhvajāḥ
ājñayā devadevasya mahādevasya śūlinaḥ
brahmāṇḍānāmasaṃkhyānāṃ brahmaviṣṇuharātmanām
na tasyeṃ karaṇaṃ kārya kriyā vā vidyate dvijāḥ
svecchayā bhagavānīśaḥ krīḍatyavijayā saha
kathitaḥ prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃkṣepānmunipuṃgavāḥ
abuddhipūrvakastveṣa brāhmī sṛṣṭirathocyate
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde prākṛtasarga kathanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
saṃvibhāgaratāḥ krūrāste parigrāhiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ
ete pañca samākhyātāḥ sargā devena bhānunā
mahataḥ prathamaḥ sargo jñātavyo brahmaṇo dvijāḥ
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūto buddhipūrvakaḥ
caturtho mukhyasargastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ
tathordhvaśrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ
tato'rvākśrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ
aṣṭamo bhautikaḥ sargo bhūtādīnāṃ dvijocamāḥ navamacaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvimeṃ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsore sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde vārāhakalpa prākṛtādisargakathanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
tataḥ sasarja bhagavāndevo'sāvātmanaḥ sutān
śaṃbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca pañcaitānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
na sṛṣṭau dadhire buddhiṃ śivaikadhyānatatparāḥ
sṛṣṭau teṣvanapekṣeṣu mohāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ
prāṇātmakaḥ samudbhūto lalāṭādbrahmaṇo haraḥ
kenāpi hetunā vimāḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ
rodayitvā'bjajanmānaṃ tasmādrudra iti smṛtaḥ
anyāni sapta nāmāni śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ
bhavaḥ śarvastatheśānaḥ paśūnāṃ patireva ca
bhīmogro mahādeva iti nāmāni sattamāḥ eit
bhūmirāpo'nalo vāyuvyoma sūrya candramāḥ
aṣṭamī dīkṣitastatra mūrtirīśasya śūlinaḥ
yābhirvyāptamidaṃ viśvaṃ viśvasyāsya jaganmayaḥ
tena viśveśvaro deva iti nāmnā śivaḥ smṛtaḥ
prajāḥ sṛjeti nirdiṣṭaścandramaulirviraścinā
sasarja manasā rudrānātmatulyānmaheśvaraḥ
nīlakaṇṭhāṃstrinetrāṃśca jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitān
vṛṣadhvajānvītarāgāñjarāmaraṇavarjitān
sarvajña śatakoṭīṃstānsarvānugrāhiṇaḥ parān
dṛṣṭvā tānvividhānrudrānviraściḥ māha śaṃkaram
jarāmaraṇanirmuktāmīdṛśīṃ mā sṛjaḥ prajām
sṛjasvānyāṃ sureśāna prajāṃ mṛtyusamanvitām
brahmāṇamabravīcchaṃbhurnāsti me tādṛśī prajā
tataḥ prabhṛti viśvātmā na prāsūta śubhāḥ prajāḥ
rudrairātmasamudbhūtaiḥ krīḍāyuktastadā'bhavat
sthāṇuvaniścalo yasmātsthitaḥ sthāṇuriti smṛtaḥ
jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvarya tapaḥ satyaṃ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ
draṣṭṛtvamātmasaṃbodho vaṣiṣṭhātṛtvameva ca
avyayāni daśaitāni nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti śaṃkare
sa eva bhagavānīśo viśveśo nīlalohitaḥ
tatastamāha bhagavānbrahmā saṃvīkṣya śaṃkaram
evaṃ viśveśvaraṃ śaṃbhuṃ samābhāṣya caturmukhaḥ
stotreṇānena tuṣṭāva śirasyādhāya cāñjalim
namaḥ śivāya devāya namaste brahmarūpiṇe
śaktirmāheśvarī tubhyaṃ tasmai vāyvātmane namaḥ
sṛjatyaśeṣamevedaṃ yaḥ svakarmānurūpataḥ
yaḥ śete śeṣaśayane viśvamāvṛtya māyayā
ātmānubhūtiyogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ
brahmāṇḍaṃ yo'khilādhāraṃ tasmai śeṣātmane namaḥ
yaḥ parānte parānandaṃ pītvā divyaikasākṣiṇam
yo'ntarā sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantā tiṣṭhatīśvaraḥ
taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ devaṃ namaste paramātmane
yasya keśeṣu jīmūtā nadyaḥ sarvāṅgasaṃdhiṣu
yaṃ vinidrā yataśvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ samadarśinaḥ
jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāstasyai yogātmane namaḥ
yasya bhāsā vibhātīdaṃ tadahaṃ tamasaḥ param
tattvaṃ sadā nirākāraṃ cidrūpaṃ pārameśvaram
yayā saṃtarate māyāṃ yogī saṃkṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
aparāntāmaparyantāṃ tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ
yaḥ śete śeṣaśayane viśvamāvṛtya māyayā
ātmānubhūtiyogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ
brahmāṇḍaṃ thoskhilādhāraṃ tasmai śeṣātmane namaḥ
yaḥ parānte parānandaṃ pītvā divyaikasākṣiṇam
yo'ntarā sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantā tiṣṭhatīśvaraḥ
taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ devaṃ namaste paramātmane
yasya keśeṣu jīmūtā nadyaḥ sarvāṅgasaṃdhiṣu
yaṃ vinidrā yataśvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ samadarśinaḥ
jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāstasmai yogātmane namaḥ
yasya bhāsā vibhātīdaṃ tadahaṃ tamasaḥ param
tattvaṃ sadā nirākāraṃ cidrūpaṃ pārameśvaram
yayā saṃtarate māyāṃ yogī saṃkṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
aparāntāmaparyantāṃ tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ
nityānandaṃ nirādhāraṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ śivam
evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ brahmā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ
prāñjaliḥ praṇatastasthau gṛṇanbrahma sanātanam
aiśvaryaṃ brahmasadbhāvaṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau haraḥ
karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca upaspṛśya maheśvaraḥ
vyājahāra mahādevaḥ so'nugṛhya pitāmaham
tvamidānīṃ mamā''deśātsṛjasva vividhāḥ prajāḥ
sargarakṣālayaguṇairnirguṇo'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ
sa tvaṃ mamāgrataḥ putraḥ sṛṣṭihetorvinirmitaḥ
bhaiva dakṣiṇādaṅgādvāmāṅgātpuruṣottamaḥ
mamaitra hṛdayādudraḥ saṃjātaḥ kāmarūpadhṛka
brahmaviṣṇuharākhyānāṃ yaḥ paraḥ parameśvaraḥ
taṃ mahāntaṃ mahādevaṃ brahmañjānanti sūrayaḥ
evaṃ brahmāṇamābhāṣya dattvā ca vividhānvarān
tataśca pāśavicchittiḥ śiva eva bhavettataḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde harotpattyādi kathanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcu kathaṃ sa bhagavānuḥ sarvasyā''dyo'pi sanvibhuḥ
sūta uvāca
āsīdekārṇave ghore naṣṭe vai sacarācare
nārāyaṇo mahāyogī śete tasmiṃstamomaye
yoganidrāṃ samāsādya śeṣāhiśayane dvijāḥ
brahmā jagāma taṃ deśaṃ yatrāssstre puruṣottamaḥ
samutthāpya ca taṃ brahmā kareṣa madhusūdanam māyayā moḍitāṃ brahmā taguṣāca sureśvaram
brūhītyukte'bravīdviṣṇurbrahmāṇaṃ tejasāṃ nidhiḥ
na jānāsi kathaṃ mūḍha māmantaryāmiṇaṃ vibhum
sarvasyā''yaṃ suraśreṣṭhaṃ jānīhītyabravīdvibhuḥ
ko bhavāniti taṃ prāha brahmā harimathābravīt
ahaṃ vai sarvabhūtānāmādyaḥ sarvajagatpatiḥ
brahmāṇaṃ māṃ paraṃ devaṃ jānīhi puruṣarṣabha
carācarātmakaṃ viśvaṃ mayi tiṣṭhati sarvadā
praviṣṭo brahmaṇo dehaṃ tatra lokāndadarśa saḥ
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ punarbrahmāṇamabravīt
carācarātmakā lokānsadevāsuramānuṣān
praviśya bhuvanānsarvāndṛṣṭvā'bhūdvismito vidhi
nāpaśyannirgamaidvāraṃ pihitāni ca catriṇā
tamabravīdgadāpāṇirbrahmāṇamamitardyutiḥ
līlārthametatsakalaṃ pitāmaha kṛtaṃ mayā
na mātsaryātsuraśreṣṭha dvārarodho mayā kṛtaḥ
tvameva jagato mānyaḥ sarvasyā''dyaḥ pitāmahaḥ
tataḥ svayaṃbhūrviśvādiśvakriṇe varamuttamam
tatastamabravīdviṣṇuṃ nā''vābhyāṃ vidyate param tvanmayaṃ manmayaṃ sarvamekā mūrtirdvidhā sthitā
evaṃ nigadito viṣṇurbrahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
kiṃ na paśyasi viśveśaṃ svayaṃjyotiḥ sanātanam
gacchāssvābhyāṃ paraṃ devamadhikaṃ śaraṇaṃ vidhe
evaṃ harernigaditaṃ śrutvā brahmā tamabravīt
āvābhyāmadhikaḥ kaścidvidyeteti mudhā hare
bhāṣase nidrayāssviṣṭastyaja mohaṃ mahāmate
viṣṇuruvāca
maivaṃ vidhe yadajñātvā paraṃ bhāvaṃ maheśvare
astīti nānyathā'haṃ te bravīmi kamalāsana
mohitātmā na saṃdeho māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ

sadā janānāṃ hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭo'pi yaḥ paraiḥ
alakṣyo lakṣayanviśvamadhitiṣṭhati sarvadā yastu kālātmayuktāni kāraṇānyapi līlayā
anantaśaktiraikātmā bhagavānadhitiṣṭhati
yasya śaṃbhoḥ parā śaktirbhāvagamyā manoharā
nirguṇā svaguṇaireva nigūḍhā niṣkalā śivā
ayamādiranādyantaḥ svabhāvādeva nirmalaḥ
anantaḥ paripūrṇaśca svecchādhīnaśvarācaraḥ
tadīyaṃ trividhaṃ rūpaṃ sthūla sūkṣmaṃ tataḥ param
asmadādyaiḥ surairdṛśyaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tu yogibhiḥ
prasādādeva sā bhaktiḥ prasādo bhaktisaṃbhavaḥ
yathehāṅkurato bījaṃ bījato vā yathā'ṅkuraḥ
tasya prasādaleśena paśoḥ pāśaparikṣayaḥ
tasmātpaśupatiḥ śaṃbhuḥ paśavastvasmadādayaḥ
sarveṣāṃ muktidaḥ śaṃbhusteṣāṃ bhāvānurūpataḥ
vālo vā taruṇo vā'tha vṛddho vā mucyate paraḥ
kaścitkṣīṇapaḍho bhūtvā punarāvartya mucyate

jñānabhāvānurūpeṇa prasādenaiva nirvṛtiḥ
tvamekā bhagavanmūrtiranyā nārāyaṇī parā
raudrī tṛtīyā kathitā jagatsaṃhārakāriṇī
etāsāṃ prerakaḥ śaṃbhuḥ svaṃ sve kārye caturmukha
nirguṇo'pi guṇādhyakṣaḥ svatantraiśvaryavigrahaḥ
tamīśvaraṃ mahādevaṃ na paśyasi kathaṃ vidhe
divyaṃ dadāmi te cakṣuryena paśyasi taṃ śivam
brahmā labdhvā paraṃ jñānamaiśvaraṃ nirguṇaṃ param
tameva śaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ
prīto bhūtvā mahādevaścaturmukhamathābravīt
tvāmeva putramicchāmi tvayā vā sadṛśaṃ sutam
tvanmāyāmohitaḥ śaṃbho na vedmi tvāṃ paraṃ śivam
namāmi tava pādābjaṃ yogināṃ bhavabheṣajam
śrutvā viraścairvacanaṃ devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk
brahmāṇamabravītputraṃ samālokyātha cakriṇam
jñānaṃ madviṣayaṃ kṣipraṃ bhaviṣyati tavānagha
eṣa yogīśvaraḥ śāṅga mamaivāṃśo na saṃśayaḥ
sāhāyye bhavitā brahmanmamā''deśāttavānagha
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ śaṃbhubrahmaṇe dvijasattamāḥ
athābravīddhṛṣīkeśaṃ prāñjaliṃ purataḥ sthitam
varaṃ varaya dāsyāmi tava nārāyaṇāvyaya
jñānajñeyātmakaṃ viśvaṃ tvanmayaṃ manmayaṃ hare
jñātā'haṃ jñānarūpastvaṃ mantā'haṃ tvaṃ matire
prakṛtistvaṃ suraśreṣṭha puruṣo'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ
tvaṃ candramā ahaṃ sūryaḥ śarvarī tvamahaṃ dinam
tvameva māyā viśvasya māyā'haṃ parama vibho
evaṃ śaṃbhorvacaḥ śrutvā vāsudevo nirañjanaḥ
abravītparamātmānaṃ mahādevaṃ dvijottamāḥ
viṣṇuruvāca
evamastvityathā''bhāṣya samāliṅganya ca śārṅgiṇam
pālayaitanmamā''deśādityuktvā'ntarhito haraḥ
tathā sarvamaśeṣeṇa kathitaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde brahma padmayonitvādikathanaṃ nāma caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
kathaṃ bhagavatī gaurī śaṃkarārdhaśarīriṇī
ṛṣaya ūcu
parabrahmātmikā nityā paramā''kāśamadhyagā
sarvaśaktimayī śāntā nirguṇā nirupadravā
svarbhābhirbhāsayantīṃ viśvametatsureśvarī
nityānandā nirātaṅkā nirvibhāgā nirañjanā

sūta uvāca
viśveśvarānmahādevādvaraṃ labdhvā pitāmahaḥ
prajāḥ sasarja bhagavānna vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ
duḥkhito'bhūttadā brahmā prajā dṛṣṭvā tu durbalāḥ
mene'kṛtārthamātmānaṃ prādurbhūtastato haraḥ
brahmāṇamabravīcchaṃbhurjñātaṃ tvadduḥkhakāraṇam
ardhanārīśvaro devaḥ svayaṃ viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ
nārī bhāgānmahādevaḥ sasarja pṛthagīśvarīm
brahmātmikāṃ parāṃ śakti koṭivālārkabhāsurām
kṣetrajñaśaktinilayoṃ paramākāśamadhyagām
brahmendraviṣṇunamitā ṣṭamūrtyaṅginīmajām
pradhānapuruṣātītāṃ sāvitrīṃ vedamātaram
ṛgyajuḥsāmanilayāmṛjvīṃ kuṇḍalinīṃ parām

sargasthityantakāriṇī vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇīm
pāhi māṃ devadeveśa śaraṇāgatavatsale
tvaṃ mātā mama kalyāṇi pitā sarveśvaraḥ śivaḥ
mṛṣṭo'haṃ tripuraghnena sṛṣṭyartha śaṃkarapriye
vividhāśva prajāḥ sṛṣṭā na vṛddhimupayānti tāḥ
tataḥ paraṃ prajāḥ sarvā maithunaprabhavāḥ kila

ekāṃ śaktiṃ bhruvormadhyātsasarjā''tmasamaprabhām

tataḥ prabhṛti viprendrā maithunaprabhavāḥ prajāḥ

sūta uvāca
asṛjadbhagavānbrahmā marīcyādīna kalmaṣān

ūrudvayāttathā vaiśyānpādācchūdrānsasarja ha

sūta uvāca
uttānapādasya suto dhruvo nāma mahāmanāḥ

sūte puṣkariṇī putraṃ cakṣuṣākṣuṣaṃ manum
tadvaṃśajā asaṃkhyātā aṅgantra tuśivādayaḥ
khyātaḥ sa pṛthivīpālo yena dugdhā vasuṃdharā

sūta uvāca
yo'sau śikhaṇḍinaḥ putro brahmacaryāśrame rataḥ

sūta uvāca
tvayaṃbhuvā samāviṣṭaḥ pūrva dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ

abravīttaṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ sarvabhūtānukampinam

sūta uvāca
